Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Love of Brothers
1 Corinthians 13:12-13
<Prayer (I)> Father, may Your love dwell in each heart, and may the eternal true human form appear throughout heaven and earth through love. We know that all creation longs to move centered around such a being. We also know that You will establish a world of brilliant culture and glory by becoming one with that true human. However, we have realized that it is a sorrow that Your love cannot dwell in us, and even when we seek that love, we cannot find it. 
Born as descendants of the fallen, we walk the historical path with the sadness that we cannot seek the connection to Your true love. Therefore, O Father of compassion, we earnestly wish for You to find us with the original heart of love and to make us children who can bow before Your heart. 
Humanity has been born as descendants of the actors in relation to You for thousands of years and has lived as a group acting in accordance with Your heart. Please allow us to confess that we have bowed before You in such a state. With compassion and love, please hold us and caress us with Your merciful hand. May this time be one where we can confess before You all our past shortcomings, unfaithfulness, and disobedience and repent sincerely.
March 31, 1968 (Sunday), at the Headquarters Church.
* This message was given during a farewell worship service held the day before sending out the leaders and active members after dividing the Seoul area churches into 10 district-level churches.

The Love of Brothers
You are the Father whom we must cherish forever. Please let us know for certain that we have an unbreakable bond with You. However, having fallen, we lost You, and our eternal connection with You has been severed, which is our sorrow. The reason we bow here today is to find the lost Father and to re-establish the severed connection with You. Yet we know that this cannot happen without Your love, so we earnestly ask that You grant us the grace of resurrection that comes from Your love. 
Bind us together through a direct relationship of love, so that we may be offered as one unified altar before You, Father. We earnestly wish for this. 
We know there are many unforgettable stories in following Your will, so we sincerely lay all our past stories before You and, in harmony with Your heart of blessing, let us deeply yearn for and admire You, and have a heartfelt desire for Your love and kindness. May we become Your sons and daughters who earnestly wish to hold Your hand and be embraced in Your bosom. On this foundation of earnest hearts, may You reign, Father, and grant us grace, allowing us to weave the bonds of life once again. Thus, may we become Your sons and daughters who receive a new mission from You and fulfill our responsibilities towards the world of hope.
Today is the last day of March. As we come to the end of the first quarter of this year, please make this day holy. Also, since today is the Sabbath, may we repent for our past failures before You and with all our hearts return to Your heart, Father. We earnestly wish for this. We believe that Your children scattered across South Korea are longing for the headquarters and worshiping today. Although their appearances may not be pleasing to You, may the overflowing heart of love among them draw the connections of heaven and earth and allow them to resurrect the many lives in the world of death. Father, we earnestly wish for this.
Please remember Your direct descendants who are scattered overseas, feeling lonely as they tread the path of pioneers. Have compassion for their loneliness. When they are sad, may You be sad with them, and when they fight, may You fight alongside them so that they can manifest the victories of the historical process in their triumphs. 
When they shed tears, blood, and sweat in the places belonging to You, that nation will surely find its way to heaven and be grafted into the foundation of resurrection. We earnestly wish for You to be present with them in that place.
Please remember the countless denominations and the many religious people, Your sons and daughters who seek goodness and yearn for the true path, and also remember the poor humanity that is exhausted from leading life in the world of death. We earnestly ask that through this day, countless spirits in the spirit world may also participate in giving joy and glory before Your grace. We entrust this entire hour to You, so please take charge of it.
We earnestly ask this, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Prayer (II)> No matter how perilous the path You walked may be, we vow not to miss a step in following You. No matter how severe the persecution You endure may be, we are already those who have offered ourselves as sacrificial offerings, so please allow us to disappear as offerings. We know that You desire to establish a foundation of life where we can connect with You amidst this world of death. We will surely establish that foundation of life.
Father, please look down upon us once again today. We long for You. We long for You immensely. We wish to live forever with You, to discuss with You, and to live while upholding Your commands. This is our wish. Since the day humanity fell, we have lived without ever being embraced in the arms of Your love even for a single day.
We know that humanity has woven a history of sorrowful tears at every turn until now, so may we become true sons and daughters who can hold on to You, who come to restore the standard of hope with the heart to seek that history once again. We earnestly wish for this.
Please allow this place to be one that the entire spirit world looks upon, and Father, may You observe this place with fiery eyes so that the bitter roots of death and sin may not remain deep within our hearts. With fiery eyes, may You help us uproot all the roots of sin today and return to You in unity, and as we humbly bow down, may You guide us. We earnestly wish for this.
May our hearts and bodies become like clay that can be molded according to Your will. For this, I must disappear, and I must have an absolute heart that can harmonize with the original nature, so I earnestly wish for You to raise that heart within us.
At this time, please take full charge.
This nation must receive love on behalf of countless peoples, and we must fulfill the mission given by You for countless tribes. As we fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us, we must become the remaining warriors in the final battle, returning the songs of victory before You and entering the final place of glory, so please directly accompany us, guide us, command us, and lead us. We earnestly wish for this.
At this time, may You alone govern this environment from beginning to end. Please do not let this become a place where the powers of darkness can intrude, nor let it become a time when wicked Satan lurks. With a heart to defend against evil and a heart that seeks only goodness, may we be able to bind this entire time before You, Father. We earnestly wish for this.
As this is the beginning time, may You govern the whole, and grant us the nature that can dissolve into Your heart in our hearts and bodies. 
All these words we offer in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Prayer (III)> Father, we must become like little children. We must be like children who cry out to You when they are hungry. A child has a yearning for their mother. That child is innocent. The more they are nurtured and cared for, the more they grow according to the standards of their parents.
Father, please remember Your children gathered here. We know that when those who have come with various circumstances lay them all bare, You cannot help but move. So, may we lay everything bare and, like a hungry child yearning for their mother’s milk, may we have a heart that longs for You, Father.
Who among us will be the teacher? They do not desire human words. They have heard many words until now, visited many churches, and met many people. However, among them, there was no honey of life, and there was no milk of life, so their hearts have been exhausted. In a desolate state, with nowhere to rely on, they are in a pitiful place, so Father, please gather them. 
They must lay aside their own circumstances and, centered on Your circumstances, the words of life and the connections of life must intertwine, and the history of re-creation where life writhes must occur.
I have not prepared to stand before You. However, I must offer all of myself before You and find myself starting from You. I must have the heart and attitude that begins from You. I must have the true form that starts from You, so I earnestly wish for You to be with me.
Having come here with a heart of sorrow for a week, Father, please comfort us, apply ointment to our wounds, and anoint us with oil, embracing us with love. So, may those who are lonely, pitiful, and tattered be granted a place in Your house where they can change their clothes and find rest. How much do You long for the sight of them going to find You with an abundance of the food of overflowing love? They also long for such a place, so we earnestly wish for You to grant it.
At this time, please take full charge and let the hearts of the one delivering the message and the one receiving it not become separate. May this become a place of empathy in tying the threads of life. We earnestly wish for You to operate this time so that our hearts and bodies can move in complete harmony, in one emotion, one heart, and may we move along one path of life. From beginning to end, we earnestly ask that You take full charge, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Words> The title of the message today is "The Love of Brothers," so I will first speak about the issue of love.
All created beings, made by God's love, exist on this earth because they began with God's love. From a single blade of grass growing by the roadside to a tiny creature living in the yard, everything was created by God's love, and you must understand this. Any artist, when creating a work, puts in their utmost sincerity with a hopeful heart. A work that is created with such sincerity and hope becomes something extremely precious to the creator, more valuable than their own life and more beloved than anything else they possess. This is undeniable when we consider the facts within our living sphere.
Therefore, we cannot say that the created world was made as a plaything or for amusement by God. No matter what object we look at, there is infinite value in it, and within all the relationships of life that flow through it, there are stories that the entire universe cannot escape. Every existence is related to great motives and processes and is connected to great purposes. We must recognize this fact. Considering these facts, we cannot deny that the created world was made within the lineage of God's love.
If there were a true person on this earth who could be with God, that is, a person who could directly receive God's love, such a person would be able to feel God's hidden love when looking at living beings, animals, or plants.
However, on this earth, there has been no true person who could love all things on this earth on behalf of the love that God had when He created all things, possessing a heart that could protect and care for all creation and share in God's joys and sorrows.
For whom did God create all things? Of course, it was for Himself, but the ultimate purpose of creating all things was for humanity. When humans become one centered on God's love, God and humanity are not two separate entities. Even if a being did not come into existence centered on a husband, when a wife completely unites with her husband centered on love, the husband and wife become one. Ultimately, the goodness of the husband and wife is not just good for one of them; it is good for all of us, and this phenomenon cannot be denied.
Since God created humans centered on love, while humans are in a relative position, if they had established a perfect position centered on God's love, God and humanity would not be two but would feel a shared value of love from the position of "we." However, has there been an ancestor who stood on such a standard? It has not appeared in the historical process until now.
Humanity's ancestors were supposed to be completely united within God's love and face all creation with the feelings and hearts of that love, but through the fall...
is why no one has been able to stand in the place of oneness with God's love until now. If it is miserable to be on the earth, there is nothing more miserable than this, and if it is pitiful, there is nothing more pitiful than this, and if it is unjust, there is nothing more unjust than this, you must understand this fact.

The reason for such a result is because of the fall. Because of the fall, true love of God cannot manifest in the human world today. Therefore, while humans discuss love and sing about happiness, there can be no happiness without God's love. Without establishing the origin of perfect love, there can be no perfect happiness.

The Center of Religious Life
The standard of perfect love has not yet emerged in the universe. A true person who can fulfill the origin of love has not yet appeared. A true parent of humanity, a man and a woman who can establish a true family centered on God's love, who can be held and loved by God, has not appeared. There has been no origin that started centered on God's love. The ancestors of humanity centered on God's love have not appeared.

Due to such a standard, humanity has fallen, leaving behind the fields and processes that should have been manifested as the ancestors of humanity. They have fallen away. Thus, it has become a sorrowful fact in the history of humanity. So what must these fallen humans seek again? Without a doubt, it is the original person. Then who is that original person? According to the Bible, it is Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity. Because humanity fell from those ancestors, to find the original standard, we must return. However, if we do not return, it is merely a dream to seek in this developed world. If we do not return, we can never find it.

What is the center of religious life? It is to devote oneself and to pray. It is to ask. Then what is the standard for praying and asking? People generally pray, "Please let our country do well." They must clearly understand that what they are currently asking for is not true. Where there is love, God cannot help but be present, and where God can love, He cannot be absent. This cannot be denied even when viewed through human life.

Because humanity started with conditions under which God cannot love, and because humanity started with conditions under which God is saddened, the history of sin has taken root, grown branches, and leaves, becoming a gnarled tree over six thousand years. You are the leaves hanging from that gnarled tree. Is that tree receiving God's love and can it be a tree that God likes? No. No matter how much that tree dreams of God's love and hopes for fruits containing God's love, such a thing can never happen.

Because such a history is latent, the world within the realm of the results of that history must be settled. It must be removed at some point. Otherwise, we cannot reach the place of true God's love that our ancestors could not attain. That is why prayer is necessary.

Some of you may have thought about what you are. Then what is a person? It is simple to say that a person is a person, but it is not that simple. A person has a body and a mind. Then what is the body? The body is made up of all elements. Then what is the mind? Buddhism says to enter a state of no-self to understand the essence of the mind. By discarding selfishness and oneself, one enters a new realm. It is said that one goes deeper and deeper into the hearts of thousands of ancestors, into the back alleys of the hearts of the ancestral grandparents of humanity. But who is in that back alley of the heart? God is there. Because we lost God there, we must go back and find Him. That is why religion starts from self-denial. A religion that starts from recognition is a doomed religion. Nowadays, some young people think that drinking and dancing and making noise is heaven, but such places are not heaven and have no relation to God's love. They are absolutely unrelated to the place where humans seek the foundation of supreme happiness.

Therefore, we must break away from such places and enter the back alley of the heart. We must enter by abandoning ourselves. We must go in alone, even if it means abandoning brothers and sisters, with the mindset that there are no ancestors or siblings in the current me. Thus, we must recall the standard of humanity's ancestors who lived with God in the beginning and reach the original standard that the ancestors of humanity, born as one man, had to establish centered on God's love. Women must also reach the original standard as women.

Restoring the position of children who have not been invaded by the fall is the foremost thing that humans must seek. Only by finding that can a new world, new relationships, and new love begin. Otherwise, one becomes a person who loves the fallen world.

People are descendants of fallen humanity. But who has seen humanity's ancestors fall? No one has seen it. However, even if one has not seen it, one can know. Just as one can know a parent by looking at a child even if one has not seen the birth, one can know by observing the world of sin. Because of the fall, no matter how much one rolls around in the world claiming to be the happiest, the heart is not at ease. Even if one claims to be in the happiest place in the world, one will eventually realize that one is among the poorest. When there are times of difficulty, one thinks of God like a god. So when one is told to prepare and eat a feast, one will be shocked and run away.

The Standard of the Righteous
So what should one have in the world to be happy and satisfied? Is it by having food? No, that will not satisfy. Then what should one have to be satisfied? There must be love. With love, even after thousands of years, one can live and eat there, soaked in love. Love remains forever. That is why the Apostle Paul said, "And now these three remain: faith, hope, and love. But the greatest of these is love." (1 Corinthians 13:13) Therefore, you must break the standard of love that deviates from the original origin of humanity and establish a new origin of cosmic history.

Then what is the fall of humanity? In general Christianity, it is said that the fall of humanity's ancestors occurred when they ate the fruit in the Garden of Eden. However, that is a comfortable interpretation. Whether it was the fruit of good and evil or a peach, or something round, does it matter? It absolutely does not. It is not acceptable to make strange and delusional stories while not having seen or tasted it and insist that it was a fruit. It is not enough to say, "When I went to Seoul, it was like this." One must know the definite starting point. Today, religious people lack a starting point. Without a starting point, the purpose is unclear, and without a clear purpose, can one explain the fall? This must be restored to the path of life through a mathematical principle, and the love that operates in this way has no relation to the fallen world.

You who are present here are people who have nothing to do with such a world and such a path, but you must understand the sorrow of the fall. You must fight against evil. Just as one side wins and the other side loses in a fight, good and evil must collide at some point, and one must break. This fighting does not stop at the individual level but must also occur in families. It cannot be avoided in society either. Thus, what has been combined has become a nation. A nation cannot unite without conflict. Therefore, the entire world has become a world of conflict.

Such fighting will become arbitrary without a certain law, so one must capture and restrain the enemy of the heart. What is needed to end the fighting? Something better is needed. If there is something better, the fighting ends. If there is something better than the enemy's, something better than the strength of the body, something better than the strength of the heart appears, then the fighting ends. Therefore, even the fulfillment of one's own desires and purposes must be restrained. In other words, without love centered on God, no matter how capable or wealthy one is, one cannot become a sacrifice. That is why those who practice the way must all go through hardships.

However, fallen humans have a strong attachment to the world. They have a strong attachment to knowledge, material, and honor. Such things are all unnecessary. In this difficult end time, what must you do? It is to fight to separate what you are most attached to. Those things prevent you from following God, so you must separate them from your practical life, and for that, you must have unwavering conviction. Also, there must be a global ideology that can crush and integrate the conflict between democracy and communism, and there must be an ideology that can change individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, allowing one to forget all worldly matters and find joy.

That is none other than God's love, but that God's love has not yet come to this earth. What do you think? Do you think many such ideologies have emerged until now? Jesus said, "For God so loved the world that He gave His one and only Son, that whoever believes in Him shall not perish but have eternal life." (John 3:16) However, love is not that simple. God's love is not simple; it is complex, and people do not understand this. No matter how much Jesus loved, He could not express a complex love. When it is said that there is no one righteous, not even one, what does that mean? It means that if there is not even one righteous person, then even Jesus could not be considered righteous. This may be disappointing to hear, but without securing a central line that can occupy the realm of complex love, one cannot fulfill God's will. That is how it is.

Complex God's Love
When teaching the principles, it is said that God's love must manifest in relative conditions, right? Love is established in relative relationships. Love cannot be established alone. Can love exist alone? Love cannot be established by denying relativity.

Then where does God's love manifest? Does it appear in God's heart? No, God's love manifests in created beings. Where does the love of a husband and wife manifest? It manifests in their children. Also, where the husband is, the love of the wife must appear. The love of the wife must also appear in the clothes the husband wears.

These days, women are quite comfortable. They use sewing machines to make clothes and borrow the strength of others. In the past, it was not like that. Even when we look at our mothers from the past, they poured their whole heart into making just one garment, one stitch at a time. That is the love of a wife for her husband. Even if we set aside love from the heart, love must manifest in life.

Just as one can know a parent's love by looking at a child, and one can know a wife's love by looking at the edge of a husband's clothing, one must be able to know God's love by observing the facts that appear in this world. But has God's love manifested? It turns out that everything is fighting and complicated; what kind of love is that? God's love must be viewed in a complex manner.

If among you, someone were to die from being struck by lightning, how unfortunate would that be? However, do not say that the Unification Church is bad because someone was struck by lightning after going to the Unification Church. If someone was struck by lightning, there must be a reason and a motive for it. The punishment occurs because the motive leads to punishment. Then what could that motive be? It is the accumulated sins from thousands of ancestors that connect and gather, bursting and breaking.

However, when one considers a person's life to be only 70 or 80 years, it seems unfair. However, if one measures it over thousands of years, everything is fair. If one accumulates good, one rises; if one accumulates sin, one falls.

Some people are blessed. However, if one receives a blessing wrongly, one will perish. If one cannot hold onto the path of blessings, one will perish. If blessings come, even if one only holds onto the tail, that becomes one's blessing, and if one rides on the head of the blessing, there is nothing to envy. Receiving blessings is because ancestors have worked hard and accumulated good deeds. It is nothing special. Without the merits of ancestors, no matter how capable you are, you will go bankrupt. Similarly, the fortune of a nation must align and follow the heavenly fortune. No matter how much a nation boasts of its greatness in the world, if it cannot align with heavenly fortune, it will inevitably go bankrupt.

You must experience God's love among all things and experience God's love in the human world. However, in the fallen world, there are mothers who do not know their children and children who do not know their mothers. That mother is that child. How can such a child cherish their mother? This world has become so corrupted. It is a world where siblings cannot stop each other from being cast out. Now this world has come to a point where it must perish. The end has come. If this troublesome world does not end soon, it must come to an end.

You will perish if you cannot make a change at this end. For example, if I can only eat Korean food and cannot eat anything else, but then all Korean food disappears, what will happen? Then, since I cannot eat anything else, I will starve. At the end, one must make a change. One must change their way of thinking to avoid indigestion. One must be able to digest even if it means swallowing a stone. One must have the digestive capacity to create nutrients from anything in the world. If one becomes such a person, one can live as long as one wants.

Even the teacher ate Japanese food when in Japan and American food when in America. However, foreigners see gochujang and run away. To them, gochujang looks ugly, but the teacher cannot express how much he missed it. When he returned to Korea, he set aside all other food and ate kimchi.

Whether in a foreign country or Korea, life is generally similar. One wakes up in the morning, has breakfast, brushes their teeth, goes to work, has lunch, comes home, and lives with their children and spouse. It is nothing special. It is just like that. However, the desire for gochujang and kimchi does not leave, whether it is day or night. It would be nice if one could make a change, but since that is not possible, one cannot live in a place where one can eat kimchi and wear traditional Korean clothes. However, at the end, one must make a change. One must change their ideology, body, and religion.

The Mother of Love
What is the central task of this world? In the past, it was clothing, food, and shelter. Clothing, food, and shelter were the center. Then where did people go? If humans were born for clothing, food, and shelter, it is truly pitiful. If one was born for a few hundred won shanty houses, it is a shocking matter, a disaster. Then for what reason were people born? People were born for the sake of people.
I was born for a true person, not for the broken and corrupted people of today. It means I was born for a true person, a true person.

Then where is the true person, and where does truth occur? To put it metaphorically, what is the greatest truth for a baby? For a baby, the greatest truth is the mother's nipple. Nothing else. Where could there be anything better than that for a baby?

Then what would be the truth at the beginning of humanity's origin? There must be something like a mother's nipple, right? That is God's love.

People wonder if God exists or not, but have you seen your heart? Is your heart round or flat? Is your heart red or yellow? You haven't seen it, right? Just because you can't see it doesn't mean there is no heart; that would be a mad person. The same goes for God. Humanity's heart is dark, so they cannot see God. God is love, love.

Now, let’s think about the origin of love. Did love start from women or from men? Have you studied this? I am a man, and if love started from women, it would be a blow to men's pride, so love must start from men, and then love would fight. Where does love start? Love arises from mothers and fathers.

You were born because of your parents' love. There is no result without a cause. The young men and women gathered here, swept away by the winds of freedom in the 20th century, shaking and making a fuss, thinking they own themselves, but all life in the universe is not yours. You must understand that there is a greater purpose of God centered around you.

Then what is the mother of love? Love is eternal, and it cannot come out against the laws of heaven and earth. Therefore, there cannot be anyone who has come out without the law of love. Love did not arise centered around any one individual. The mother of love is God's love. Even if siblings fight, they become peaceful when they see their mom and dad. Likewise, there must be a mother of love in the human world. However, when you look at human love or love in the universe, there is no mother of love. Originally, there was one, but humanity has lost it. What humanity has lost is precisely God's love. Therefore, today, the noun love is fighting centered around your hearts. The boundary is astonishing. When you see this, you cannot deny that human love has fallen.

That is why the sign that says "God is love" has been put up. When God loves like this, what does it mean? It means to love one another. When He gave His only begotten Son, this only begotten Son cannot be seen merely as one person. You must understand that the only begotten Son appeared because he received God's love in this way. God is love. However, that does not mean God equals love. Although God is omniscient and omnipotent, God does not equal omniscience and omnipotence. It merely indicates that it is the center.

When you love, can you do it without knowing God, the source of love? God is the root of love; can you, the leaves, love without knowing the root? For example, if a poplar leaf says, "The root is bothersome. The stem is bothersome," can it exist? The root must exist for the stem and leaves to exist. However, if the east wind blows and it wants to fly west, it is doomed. The root of the tree must exist for the leaves to cling tightly. Only then can the leaves stay attached at the top of the tree without falling off. What power is greater than the power of the root that clings tightly? It is the profound love of God. That love of God governs life. Love without roots is shaky.

However, fallen humanity was born from rootless love, so it shakes and turns without roots. It walks on a path that is not a wide road but a precarious cliff, where taking a single step becomes sin. There is no root of love in the human world.

Because the motive of true love did not come out, the foundation of individual hearts has been distorted, and because the foundation of individual hearts has been distorted, the foundation of families has been distorted, and the society formed around distorted families has also been distorted, and the foundation of nations connected to such societies has been distorted, and everything in the world formed by such nations has been distorted. In order to restore this distorted foundation, humanity must recreate love like that of a mother's love. If it cannot be done, it must be recreated even at the cost of oneself, even if the nation falls and the world falls.

When God's kingdom is established, the term judgment has emerged on earth. You must pass through the gateway of judgment. If there are worries left in your personal lives, pain left in your families, pain left in society, pain left in your nation, and pain left in the world, how will you pass through this gateway of judgment? To pass through there, a lawyer must come forth.

Therefore, there were those who took on the responsibility of a lawyer, saying, "I will defend in this regard," and who were they? They are the founders of religions who have come and gone until now. Among them, the one closest to us is Christianity. Christianity calls God the Father centered on love, calls Jesus the Bridegroom, and calls the people of the world the Bride. And the religion that has dug into the process of human life centered on love is Christianity. The conclusion is that Christianity could not help but become a global religion because God is alive. However, if you can be a husband who can defend, saying, "My wife is the best," and a parent who can defend, saying, "Our children are the best," how wonderful would that be? Then God would also be pleased.

God has hoped for a protagonist who can defend all humanity as an individual until now. He also hoped for a family that could defend before the world in conflicting positions. And He has given the responsibility of defending on behalf of tribes, nations, and all humanity to that family. Thus, it is to establish God's kingdom.

When that kingdom is established, all of humanity will become the chosen people. Moreover, everything governed centered on that kingdom will become the ideology of the chosen people.

The one who came to conclude this world is the Lord, the Savior. The Savior is the one who takes responsibility for our defense in the courtroom of individual judgment. He takes us out from the courtroom of families, tribes, nations, and the world. He takes us up. And if there is a family that can say, "I will go even to the place of death," it can return to the home of restored love while singing songs of restoration, how wonderful would that be?

Christians have the responsibility to revive the world. They must walk the path of sincerity in place of the shepherd of the wilderness. Because you were born with the bloodline of evil, you must have the conviction to stake your life to eliminate it. You must empty your hearts to have only true love. When you delve into true love, you find that I am there, and my mother is there, and my father is there. There is also a wife and children.

You must find the root of true love. If there is a family that can sprout from that root on the ground, it can dominate the world. When love sprouts from that family, the culture of humanity's ancestors begins to be created. The language used there becomes the language of the world. It does not matter what language is currently in use. English will be judged one day.

If you want to be a child, you must be born through parents who have true love in a society of love and learn the language they speak. Thus, you must start toward a new world through that nation. From there, a culture centered on love will develop. That culture will become a global culture, and other cultures must pass through that land. The culture of that place will be the culture that represents the world.

The thought of the Second Coming, as expressed in Christianity, has emerged to create such a world. There is no religion without the thought of the Second Coming. This is because the people of this earth have lost the root of love. That is why the Bible refers to all people as orphans. When an orphan goes to a palace where nobles live, it turns out to be a den of enemies, and instead of eating good food, they are consuming drugs mixed with poison, and instead of dancing joyfully, they are dancing on the edge of a blade.

Therefore, you must find the root of love. That is, you must find God's love. Paul said, "Faith, hope, and love, these three remain, but the greatest of these is love." (1 Corinthians 13:13) Everyone, what is faith? If you write the character for faith in Chinese, it is '信.' If you take away the character for 'person' (人) from it, only the character for 'word' (言) remains. Ultimately, faith means the words of a person. At this time, words signify the relationship between people. If there is no relationship, there can be no words, so when you speak, it already becomes a relative standard. Moreover, for a relationship to be established, there must be faith (信).

Where does this foundation come from? It comes from the connections forged by love. However, those connections were not made arbitrarily. They were made because there were conditions of power for the connections to be made and the standards of the intended purpose could align with each other.

What is our wish? Is it to find people, or is it to find truth? It is to find the true embodiment of truth. When true people and true truths become one, hope is fulfilled, and faith is established. Then what remains? It is love. We must successfully overcome the peak of love. Faith, hope, and love will always exist, and among them, the greatest is love, so everything must be achieved centered on this love.

However, fallen humanity hopes to find true truth. Thus, they aim to form a true view of life, a true worldview, and a true cosmology, centered around that to create a new world on earth. That central ideology is precisely the thought of the Messiah.

History is a journey toward finding true truth. That truth must present the way for true individuals to live, for true families to live, for true societies to be formed, for true nations to be established, and for true worlds to be realized. Thus, the focus from individuals to the world must all align for the completion of the world, the completion of nations, the completion of tribes, the completion of families, and the completion of individuals to be possible. The one who brings the core words, that is, the truth that can align like this, is the Messiah, and that truth is God's true love.

However, until now, humanity has gone wrong in moving toward a new world because they did not know the truth. Therefore, if there is someone who starts to find the true cosmology and teach true life, they must embark toward a new world, centered on that person, receiving God's love. This is the means to establish the heavenly kingdom on earth.

The Lord who is coming has the original true love of God and the true truth of God. Through this truth, families are opened, societies, nations, and the world are opened, and individual, familial, tribal, national, and global love, ideology, and personality are initiated. These things start from individuals. Therefore, a person who lives truly as an individual is someone who lives for the world, no matter where they are on the ends of the earth. In the world of love, that is the case.

Living one hour in the world of heart can be a source of pride for a thousand years, and living one day can be a source of pride for ten thousand years, allowing one to experience the preciousness of life. That love is true love. Have you ever felt such true love? You must be certain that true love exists. True love can even feel the energy of cells expanding. That world is a world where God's love exists. It is a world that is difficult to express in words, but it gives a feeling like flying on a cloud on a sunny spring day, a world where every cell feels like it is dancing.

You must receive the eternal essence that allows you to live such a wonderful life from God. Even though there is God's love available to supplement this, some people always live in a place where they do not know God's love.

Therefore, no matter how much the people of the world slander and persecute the Unification Church and its founder, I will go the way I must go, even if it means death. Even if my legs are cut off or my spine is broken, I can endure such things. Even if I am told to dance in dirty water, I can do it. I can wash it clean with clear water. Even if I take on all the slander of the world and carry the burden of insults, it is okay. Insults do not provide nourishment, so they do not fill the stomach, but one must know how to digest insults as if they were nutrients.

The teacher has always been alone. There are many signs persecuting the Unification Church. They even call the Unification Church the International Communist Party. We were persecuted by the Japanese during the colonial period and by the communists in the North. Recently, somewhere, they even said the Unification Church is affiliated with the Chochongryun. It is absurd, but I said, "I will bear it all without saying a word. If I am insulted, it is fine as long as South Korea is blessed." However, they say to kill the teacher. What will be the aftermath? The most terrifying thing for the members of the Unification Church is losing the teacher. There is nothing more precious to you than the teacher. Everyone, is that right? "Yes." Even if you lose your husband, it may be okay, but you must not lose the teacher of the Unification Church. That is why the Unification Church is great.

People in the world say all sorts of insults, claiming that the teacher of the Unification Church performs some kind of magic. Once, in order to drive out the communists, I crossed over to the North, but I ended up getting captured. Just because I came from the South, they called me a lackey of Syngman Rhee. However, no matter how much they investigated, they could not find any evidence. So they imprisoned me, saying I was a shaman and that I was disturbing society. The teacher has been beaten a lot. I have suffered a lot of torture and endured a lot of humiliation. These days, my health has improved a lot, but I am a person who has walked that path. There have been many dramatic scenes. When I think of those as precious times to achieve a hopeful tomorrow, they become valuable moments.

During the colonial period, I was beaten so much that I sometimes fainted for hours. However, I do not yield to the whip. A person who cannot love their country cannot love God absolutely. When I first went to Japan, the people loyal to the Japanese imperial family looked down on me and rebelled, but after 20 years, I returned and gathered all the Japanese youth. Now, whatever I demand, they will listen. The Unification Church has grown larger due to the insults. But how much larger would it have grown if it had not been insulted?

Those who are here for the first time may not know much about the Unification Church. However, if the teacher's story were woven into a drama and broadcast for just three days, even the most stone-hearted person would weep. Conscience is felt through conscience, and connections are felt through connections, so those with good character will feel it.
When you come to understand the meaning of the Unification Church, it becomes strange. You lose interest in worldly studies. This is because your objects of interest change. Those with purpose have a lot of interest in the Unification Church. The teacher does not meet anyone domestically, but when he goes abroad, it is different. The teacher meets everyone he wants to meet. He discussed for over an hour that meeting President Eisenhower and declaring a ceasefire in Korea in 1953 was a mistake. He might meet again when he goes to America this time. Just because he is threatened not to come, will he not go? What about you? "I will go." The answer is clear, but it is not an easy thing as it sounds.

The teacher has been alone without a single friend until now. Even when he went to North Korea, there was no counterpart. He has always been alone. Even now, he is alone. Although you may follow the teacher subtly, it is to set up your own success, not for the teacher. It is always about yourselves first. If you feel bad, you complain about it. When there is a blessing, you say, "Teacher, our son is three years old; can you not bless him? Why are you leaving our son out?" Who are you believing for? It is not for the teacher; it is for yourselves. That is why the teacher is alone.

True Love
The true itself cannot be established without the arrival of a true person. The true itself is fundamentally different from falsehood. The true does not desire false people and cannot give true love to false people. Since Unification Church members deal with the most true things, there must be love. However, the love of God, the Lord of the universe, has not yet been revealed. Therefore, we must seek and establish that love of God. Thus, we aim to correct the deviated path and to grasp the root of true love. That is our hope.

You may wonder if you can experience God's love in the Unification Church. The Unification Church has many differences from ordinary churches. It is said that once you enter the Unification Church, you cannot leave because it is like an electric field. That is true. But the electricity is the electricity of God's love. Although electric lights, lamps, shades, and insulators are visible, the actual electricity is invisible. When a person gets attached to this invisible electricity, they die. The electric current of God's love is also invisible. No matter how much you move, think, or read books, you cannot know it. Love cannot be explained theoretically. What is established by theory can be created by humans.

Until now, humanity has developed scientific civilization by applying theories, and similarly, if there is a theory of love recognized by the spirit world, it means that love can also be created by humans. In other words, love is something that cannot be thought of by the human brain and exists in a different dimension. It transcends all concepts and notions.

For this reason, true love cannot be established in the fallen world. In the end, it is about sorting out the love of the fallen world. Therefore, the great judgment refers to uprooting the roots of the wicked world that have existed until now, cutting off the trunk, and grafting in the original love. To graft, it must be cut off, right? Because the time for such a great judgment has come, all laws of families are breaking apart. Globally, everything is breaking apart. Fallen world humans do not know their children, parents, society, or country; they only know "me, me, me," so they must awaken.

America is in big trouble. They thought democracy was good, but individualism has spread, leading to separation and destruction. Individualism will fail. If the nation is failing and one just sits idly by, the nation will perish, and the idea that as long as I live well, it doesn't matter what happens to society is bound to fail. Such things do not exist in the heavenly way. This individualistic ideology is the cause of America's chaos. So how do we turn this around? Correcting and fixing these things is the Unification thought.

The love that has existed until now has been established by Satan and must be settled. Since fallen humanity has no concept of love, we must plant the love centered on God. Does a parent need to explain their love for their child? Is theory necessary? Does a husband love his wife theoretically? Love cannot be communicated through theory and explanation. What is love that one lives and dies for? Logic and theory are useless in this matter. You need God's love, and you want to find the root of that love.

So where does God's love manifest? If it only appears in God Himself, it has nothing to do with humanity, and even the millennium kingdom is useless. God's love is manifested in people. Originally, if humanity had not fallen, God's love would have been revealed to the first ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve. Is love something that sleeps when evening comes? Is it something that, when the time comes, one packs up and leaves with regret? The love you know may be like that.

God's love is manifested in people.
Even fallen people in this world, when they wake up in the morning and see their beloved child's face dirty, do not mind it. Even if they haven't brushed their teeth, they still hug and kiss them because they are so lovable. Mothers find it amusing to see their babies suckle so hard that they draw blood. They feel good even as they are taking away their own flesh and essence. They just look down at them lovingly. When the baby asks for milk at night, they first taste it before giving it. Isn’t that right, ladies? If a mother doesn't do that, she is a fake mother.

When a mischievous child goes outside, fights, cries, and makes a fuss, and then returns home, the parents' hearts ache immensely. Why is that? It is because the physiological nature of a person makes them love their child so much. The love of that nature manifests in actions that transcend time and space. Similarly, when Unification Church members are insulted, the teacher's heart aches. This is because he cannot help but love you as a parent.

If parents oppose the love of their sons and daughters, saying, "Do not love again," is that right? No, it is not. Their love is absolute. The more someone tells them not to, the more they do. "If we can't live on this earth, let’s live together in the next world," they say, and they die for it. This is the disorderly character of the world. Humans must follow the laws of order. Therefore, we must have a revolution centered on love.

However, if a greater love emerges than the love of the satanic world, the love of the satanic world will decline. No matter how much a husband cries and tells his wife not to go, if there is a greater love, she will go there. No matter how much the husband hits her, or how much the wife says she cannot live without him, she will go. A person who has tasted God's true love cannot live anywhere else. This is the motivation behind the Unification Church being insulted. Is that a sin or a virtue? Once you taste something delicious, no matter how expensive it is, you will want to eat it, right? Similarly, if there is a greater love than the love they like, their hearts will gravitate toward that love. The Unification Church promotes this well, doesn’t it? (laughter) When you enter the Unification Church, such things happen, so both husbands and wives must come in. If a husband goes to the Unification Church, the wife should quickly follow and kneel down. Only then will something unprecedented in history happen.

What is love? It is to believe. Therefore, we must be grafted onto the one and only love. That is why Jesus said, "Follow me. I am the only begotten Son of God." When true love, greater love, appears, it must be connected to that love. The essence of love does not change.

God's love is manifested in humans. But does God's love appear first in men or women? Where should it first appear? Women will say it should first appear in women, and men will say it should first appear in men, and they will argue. So we must think about this. When God created humans, who did He create first? He created Adam first. Adam is Adam because he is Adam. (laughter) Did God create Adam to play around with him? When you think about it, the features of a person's face are created in perfect harmony. All human emotions are meant to be expressed on that face. Therefore, you can know everything by looking at a face. Smiling is good, and crying is good. However, joy and sorrow are different. When one is happy, the face turns red. If a person can govern their sorrow, their life will change. What is sorrow? It is pain. One must be able to govern pain. After that, one must govern money. One must become a person who can think of money as just a piece of paper and overcome it.

When you are sad, do you cry or not? "I do." Yes, you all resemble me. (laughter) It is because you resemble God. God is like that too.

The Love of the Servant to Be Settled
There is a good lesson for us Unification Church members, and that is the concept of indemnity. 

With just these two characters of indemnity, even if I wear a crown and die, I will establish conditions of indemnity for humanity. Would that be a grievance? How great is the principle of indemnity in the Unification Church? Is the Unification Church still a heresy? Creating hope through the steps of being insulted and driven away is the return through indemnity. Even in a position of being insulted and driven away, I must think that by walking this path, all people receive indemnity. That cannot be an easy task.

The path to your rebirth is the path of suffering and fear. Therefore, you must feel joy there and seek hope. Because you have hope, even if there are some hardships and sad things, you must overcome them. A great person is someone who overcomes all pain and sorrow while seeking new hope, striving to understand the flow of cosmic and historical events to bless humanity. The teacher aims to make Unification Church members such people.

The teacher has spoken for 11 hours and 45 minutes before. That was a miracle. However, even after talking for such a long time, no one left saying it was long and boring. Everyone, where did I say God's love is manifested? I said it is manifested in people. Then how does God's love manifest? It appears according to the order of love. First, the love of parents, then the love of spouses, and then the love of children. Until now, I have wanted this to manifest in the Unification Church. There is one more thing to add, and that is the love of siblings. The love of siblings adds value to me, and from now on, love is promised.

Humans have not achieved true parental love, true spousal love, or true children's love since the beginning of history. Until now, humanity has practiced fallen love. We should start centered on God's supreme love, but due to the fall of the human ancestors, we started centered on the love of the archangel, who is a servant of God. It started from the love of a servant.

Do you want to receive the love of a servant or the love of a master? You must receive the love of a master. Until now, you have received the love of a servant. You have received an incomplete love. Therefore, should you settle that, or should you hold onto it? You must settle it.

The archangel lured the ancestors of humanity and violated the laws of love. God's hope is to cut off the ties of the fallen history of suffering over the past 6,000 years. God's heart wanted to execute fallen humanity into the chaos of the dark universe, but why did He not do so and left them? It was because of the parental love that wanted humans to shed the shell of the fall through their own laws and return to their original position.

Since humans have fallen into the position of a servant of a servant, to find their original position, a true servant of God must emerge. The teacher bears that responsibility, which is why he is trying to make you true servants of God. You must become true servants of God.

Because there is a standard that humans are the children of the archangel, they must re-establish a loving relationship with God and become representatives of heavenly servants. Therefore, you must be loyal to God and become a servant whom God can love. After that, you must become adopted children. You must return as adopted children. What is the difference between adopted children and direct descendants? It is the bloodline. Nowadays, everyone can only become adopted children.

An adopted child is needed when there is no direct child or when a child exists but has become a delinquent or has betrayed the parents. Since God has no direct daughters, He needs adopted children and adopted daughters. God cannot trust the children of servants, but since He has no sons or daughters, He must take the children of servants and create adopted children.

Therefore, the Israelite nation is adopted. That is why they called God "Abba Father." They call Him "Abba Father" in the name of an adopted child. Because they are adopted, they cannot directly call God their Father. They have a father who gave birth to them, and there is also God.

What the Unification Church Teaches
Originally, Adam and Eve were created as God's direct children, but they were led away by a servant and committed sin, receiving the blood of a servant and becoming the offspring of a servant. Thus, the children of God became children destined to perish.

This is why the Unification Church is persecuted and chased away. The Unification Church is insulted by established Christians not because they are inferior. Some people say that the leader of the Unification Church dances naked, but tell them to stop talking nonsense. Do not speak like a sleepwalker. The leader of the Unification Church is not that kind of frivolous man. If I were to crumble under such words, I would have packed up long ago. How long can I live? Even though I look like this, I was the top wrestler in high school. If I wanted to take revenge on them, I could do it. I could finish it in one blow. But why can’t I? Because we have the mission of world restoration. At this turning point, I have endured until now. Regardless of what others say, I am working while going back and forth openly. No one in the world can do this except the teacher.

For whom did God lose His son? In Genesis, it says it was because Adam and Eve ate the forbidden fruit. Because God's sons and daughters fell and became the children of servants, He had to take the children of servants and raise them. How much must God have lamented? Everyone, think about it from a different perspective. You must understand this to become God's direct children.

Today, Christians cry, saying God is omniscient, omnipotent, and holy, but they are people who find it hard to receive blessings. Because the original sons and daughters fell, they must indemnify the 6,000 years of human history that has been disrupted. However, Christians do not realize that they are in a position to create conditions to teach and nurture the children of servants to establish God's son, and instead, they say, "God, give us blessings." They must return blessings before receiving blessings.
From here on, the world has a different origin, and next, you will change. Before I can be liberated from God, I must first liberate God. As children, we must love our parents, yet we ask God for blessings instead? We must repent for our unfilial actions and relieve the deep sorrow that resides in the heart of our Father. Even if I am whipped and cast aside before all people, I must remember that it is the duty of a filial child to go forth. This is what the Unification Church teaches.

What is right, everyone? Should we unconditionally say, "Oh, please bless me," because we need blessings? If so, then everyone becomes a thief, everyone becomes Cain. Without understanding the heart of our parents, we become like the offspring of servants, asking our parents for our share. Do we know our place when we say such things?

Why does the great King of the heavenly world lose all His sons and daughters and get dragged into the world of servants to find them? It is because humanity has been dragged into being the servants of servants. That is why Satan repeatedly mocks and spits before God, causing repeated ruin. When Satan takes humans away, God brings them back, and who knows the tangled story of 6,000 years? The relationship of being servants of servants has been repeated, and now we must settle this and elevate it to the relationship of adopted children, to the relationship of sons, so that we may inherit the great work of heaven and earth all at once. Who can understand God's tremendous inner heart?

To become God's legitimate child, God has had love for servants and love for adopted children until now, but He has never loved a legitimate child. Therefore, to establish God's love for legitimate children among all people on this earth, He sent one person, and that person is His only begotten Son, Jesus. Thus, centered on the relationship with Jesus, the wild olive tree of humanity must cut off all its branches and be grafted onto the true olive tree, which is Jesus. This is the history of restoration.

How many historical processes has the whole universe gone through in anticipation of that one person? Yet, that Jesus faced persecution on this earth, which is such a lamentable and heartbreaking matter. Humanity has killed such a son, and they have remained as wild olive trees.

Therefore, for the Lord to come again, He must bring the noun of unity so that the circumstances of Jesus and our desire for the Lord to come align. Only then does it fit into the truth. And the Lord must come again to marry. We must not block the spiritual world. The spiritual world is the root of the physical world.

The Lord, who has become the true olive tree, must come again so that all humanity can be grafted from Him, reaching the positions of adopted children and legitimate children. Let’s Become Those Qualified to Speak  
I wanted to spend time with you during the training period, but I regret that I could not attend due to various circumstances.  
The significance and characteristics of this training session  
This year marks the first year of the second 7-year course, and this training session you received is the first one since entering 1968, and it is the first training session held after the completion of the first 7-year course, so I believe it holds significant meaning. For this reason, the teacher wanted to spend a lot of time with you, and since you came to the headquarters, you probably thought there would be many opportunities to meet the teacher, but I regret that it did not happen.  
Now you must return the way you came after finishing the training session. However, your feelings about returning now will be quite different from when you came to the training session. And in your homes or regions, those waiting for your return will be looking forward to you.  
Unlike before, we invited many external speakers to this training session. This is because our Unification Church has established a certain level of face in external activities, and they are seen as standing on a standard that they can recognize. Therefore, by inviting such people to give lectures, we aimed to gain double benefits.  
Our trainees must have some standards they admire and aspire to. And those who have not graduated from university must have envied the scholars and doctors at the university, thinking how wonderful they must be. How great it would be to graduate from university! They must have thought. By inviting prominent figures from Korea and listening to their lectures, you will have many results from comparing, criticizing, observing, and probing yourselves. Thus, you will have evaluated them from our perspective. How precious is the very position from which you can evaluate the standards they present? And how precious is the ideology we possess? I believe you have thought a lot about this.  
Another benefit is that we introduced the movements of the Unification Church to those people. Professor Lee, Hang-nyung had planned and prepared everything to lecture here, but it seems he was not very pleased at first when he saw your appearances. I heard that he could not say everything he wanted to. However, during his lecture, he realized, "Oh! I was wrong." Although we appeared shabby before him, he felt that there was a significant difference between his knowledge standard or the current social knowledge standard and the personal standards we possess.  
At first, he thought of us as nothing based on his own thoughts, but during the lecture, he controlled himself and reevaluated himself. This realization must have been a great lesson for him. The fact that he felt this way will come to mind whenever he attends any meeting or stands in any official capacity.  
He initially thought that the youth of the Unification Church were nothing when viewed externally, but after seeing the content of their questions, he thought, "These young people have grown." Therefore, whenever he stands in any official capacity looking at the public, the image of the Unification Church trainees will come to mind. Considering this, I believe we provided him with good material this time.

Purpose of Inviting External Speakers  
In light of this, you should understand that the issue is not about the prepared environment but about what kind of background it has and what facts emerge through that background, meaning that the current appearance is not the problem.  
From this perspective, the professors who visited this time will not casually evaluate that "the Unification Church was like this or that." They must have felt something different from what they have felt on the podium until now. The more they feel such things, the more they will talk about the Unification Church whenever religious issues arise, as they have dealt with the best people in the Republic of Korea.  
Since they have relationships that can deal with high-ranking individuals, it will be beneficial for us to seek ways to indirectly proclaim our Unification Church through those people in the future. Therefore, we have tried this this time, and in the future, we plan to invite influential figures from all walks of life.  
The content they lectured on this time is the essence of their specialized fields of study. They learned all of this in just an hour and a half or two hours. If we were to publish a book, we could invite about 20 people to give lectures. Collecting what they lectured on would make a good book.  
When people stand on a podium, they tend to want to boast about themselves and present the best part of their expertise to the public. Therefore, the content they lecture on is likely to be the best they can assert.  
Until now, we have been one-sided in faith, but now we have grown to the extent that we can interact socially with such people. We invited such people to listen to their lectures, believing it would greatly benefit you, which is why we invited external speakers this time.  
Now, after just one night, you will return to your respective homes. What will you say when you return? When a person returns from a trip, they must bring a gift. So, what will you say as a gift to make those waiting for you happy?

The harmonious spring 
Spring is also a season of harmony. During the tedious winter, we felt a great distance between heaven and earth. However, with the arrival of spring, heaven lowers, and the earth rises, making it feel as if the distance has narrowed.
