Let Us Comfort Heaven
All human beings living on this earth today are searching for the center of comfort. They are seeking personal comfort, familial comfort, national comfort, and global comfort. Furthermore, they are searching for a universal center of comfort that represents the entire heaven and earth. This is an undeniable fact.
The Need for a Center of Comfort
As long as heaven and earth exist, there must inevitably appear a being who becomes the center of comfort. That being must become the subject of comfort and be able to comfort all people. It must comfort individuals, families, nations, and the world to create a world of hope. God has established the thought of the Messiah in front of humanity to send such a being and has led the providential history up to now. Given this fact, you cannot deny the existence of God.
Therefore, the one who comes as the center of comfort cannot simply end as a personal being of comfort; a family representing the whole must emerge centered on that being, and a tribe must emerge, and a nation must arise. This is the concept of the chosen people that has appeared in the historical process on this earth. Jacob laid the foundation of Israel by overcoming evil, and it was from that foundation that the sprouts of comfort began to emerge centered on God. From that family, if a tribe of comfort, a nation of comfort, is established, then the standard of a global nation of comfort will finally be established. You must understand that the one who came before that national standard was the Messiah.
For this overall responsibility, in other words, to move this world, which is filled with sorrow and loneliness, into a world of comfort and peace, Jesus came to this earth. Had that nation, which was prepared at that time, completely united with Jesus, humanity would have finally been able to find the origin of peace that they had longed for in their hearts, and all people would have met the subject of comfort and seen the beginning of happiness. However, since they could not accept Him when He came, we must recognize that this is one of the most sorrowful facts in the historical process up to now.
Thus, humanity must have a center of comfort. A nation, a tribe, a family, and an individual must emerge as a central being that can connect to the nation and the world. Without this, you must understand that a heavenly kingdom of comfort cannot possibly be established on this earth.
Adam and Eve, Who Could Not Be Objects of God's Comfort
From God's perspective, if humanity had not fallen, Adam and Eve growing in their own right would have been objects of comfort before God, and all of creation would have been objects of comfort before God. Everything they moved and lived with would have become stimulating elements of comfort before God. However, because humanity fell, you must understand that God could no longer have that one individual who was an object of comfort. In this regard, it can be seen that humanity is not the only one searching for the object of comfort; God is also seeking an object of comfort.
How can we comfort God? To comfort God, we must understand what kind of beings Adam and Eve were. Adam and Eve were established to fulfill all of God's will. In other words, Adam and Eve were created as the center of all God's joy and happiness, capable of relating to it. How good must it have been for God to see such Adam and Eve? At the same time, you must think about how much God wanted to share His stories and feelings with them, centered on that ideal to fulfill His original will.
Because Adam and Eve fell, God could no longer regard them as true ancestors of humanity, as parents of humanity, or as His sons and daughters. Even though Adam and Eve were God's one and only children, they ended up standing in a position where God could not treat them as His children. After Adam and Eve matured, God intended to bless them as a couple and make them objects of comfort. However, they could not become objects of comfort as His sons and daughters, nor could they become objects of comfort as a bride and groom.
God had a great desire for them, granting them infinite value, but because they fell, He could not feel the heart of comfort as a parent, nor could He feel the heart of comfort as a husband and wife. God wished for Adam and Eve to become ancestors of hope in the future, to stand as a king before all humanity, and to establish the duty of loyalty and filial piety before Him. However, you must understand that they could not become objects of comfort before God.
To Comfort God
So, how can we comfort such a God? Based on the standard of fallen Adam and Eve, we cannot become objects of comfort before God. Since we could not stand before Him as true sons and daughters, we must become true sons and daughters to comfort God. Since we could not stand as true husband and wife, we must stand as true husband and wife to become objects of comfort. As a central figure who can govern heaven and earth, and as a king who can govern nations or all people, Adam and Eve must fulfill their responsibilities; otherwise, no matter how much we try to comfort God, it cannot be true comfort.
For this reason, someone must come to this earth bearing this responsibility of comfort. If there is no one to bear that overall responsibility, then at least an individual must appear. If there are no sons, then at least a daughter must come. While we should have both sons and daughters, at least one must exist.
However, because the ancestors of humanity fell, and without passing through the principle of re-creation, they cannot be restored, a man must first emerge. A woman cannot appear without a man. No matter how much she wants to comfort God as His daughter, if a man does not come first, a woman alone cannot fulfill the responsibilities of a daughter. For this reason, until now, those who have borne the responsibilities of the providential history of restoration have not been women but men.
Then, what were the men supposed to do when they came to this earth? They were to restore the standard that Adam could not fulfill in comforting God and could not fulfill as a true son, and to connect humanity with God. You must understand that our ancestors have come and gone bearing this historical responsibility.
Since this world is an evil world governed by Satan, when those who bear such responsibilities appear, they must organize this world centered on them and dismantle the world of Satan. Therefore, from the family of Adam through Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus, and throughout the long historical course of 6,000 years, those who have borne the will of heaven have been men, not women. Thus, on the foundation of all the devotion offered by these responsible men, a true son must emerge. A person must appear whom God can say, "You are my beloved son."
The one who came to this earth as such a central being was Jesus. When Jesus was baptized by John the Baptist at the Jordan River and came up out of the water, the voice of God was heard saying, "This is my beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased." (Matt 3:17) This meant that heaven and earth had finally found a being in whom they could rejoice. You must understand how great God's joy was in this.
The Center of God's Comfort is the Greatest Son
Then, what kind of object of comfort should Jesus be before God? He must fulfill the mission of a son who can comfort God from a position that transcends the sorrowful history affected by Satan. Therefore, when God looks at Jesus, He must not have the impression that He is a restored second son of fallen descendants, nor should He leave the impression that He is a son who has caused God much suffering. He must be a son whom God can call "You are my beloved, my well-pleasing one." In other words, He must become the subject of comfort as the greatest son on this earth, and His value must exceed that of Adam and Eve before the fall.
Since God created Eve through Adam, a son must be welcomed for a woman to appear. However, when Jesus came to this earth and stood as a son before God, He could not find a being who could stand as a daughter before God. Therefore, it was necessary to find such a being, which is the concept of the bride.
What has God labored for over the past 6,000 years? While He has prepared the external foundation for victory to save the world, He has not saved the world. Therefore, while God has been laying the external foundation, internally, He had to establish the standard that Adam and Eve should have achieved in the Garden of Eden without falling. In other words, He had to establish the standard of the object of love and the object of comfort within God's original heart. If this is not achieved, this world cannot be restored. Therefore, to establish this, God raised the Israelite people.
Thus, God established Jacob and made him suffer for 21 years in Haran, and on his way back home, He made him wrestle with an angel at the Jabbok River. Here, the angel symbolized Satan. This fight was to determine whether Jacob, who was bearing the responsibility of restoration, could win against the angel to restore the heavenly order that had been disrupted by the archangel. It was a fight between Jacob and the angel to remove the sorrow that had been bound in God's heart. After wrestling all night, Jacob said, "I will not let you go unless you bless me," and if he had heard the angel say that it could not be done, could the nation of Israel have possibly come forth?
In Jacob's journey home, winning the fight against the angel meant he could go home; losing meant he could not, so it was a battle of life and death. The moment Jacob fought to leave a blessed lineage, or in other words, to leave a blessed bloodline, was a moment where everything was at stake, a battle of life and death.
The moment Jacob wrestled with the angel was a moment where all the faith and heart he had accumulated over 21 years collided. How weary must Jacob have been from the trials he faced? Hadn't Laban deceived him over ten times and made his life difficult by giving him his daughter? Breaking free from such an environment, he said, "Are you blocking my path? No matter how much you have the greatest energy and strength..."
was determined to set the standard for victory, saying, "Even if I am losing, will you be able to defeat me?" Did he act like you all, watching the situation and being cautious? No, he did not care about such things. Since they fought for a decisive battle, it was inevitable that the angels would bless them. Did they do it out of joy? No, they did it because they had no choice but to do so.

From this origin, Satan was separated, and in the sense of having achieved victory, they received the blessing of Israel. Thus, from Jacob as an individual and Jacob's family, a tribe was formed, and that tribe must be a victorious tribe. A blessed tribe cannot all fall into ruin. A victorious tribe is different.

Then what is the purpose of being blessed to achieve victory? Is it for their own prosperity? That is a misunderstanding. The Israelites, whom God loves and blesses, must prosper because they are a nation loved by God, unlike the Gentiles.

What is the purpose for which God established the nation of Israel? What was the purpose of blessing Israel? It was to send a son who could be the object of God's comfort, and to unite completely around that son. Contrary to Jacob's struggle with the angel at the Jabbok River, it was to receive the protagonist who could establish the homeland.

If the protagonist, Jesus, went to the mountain, and they followed him to the mountain; if he went to the sea, and they followed him to the sea, what would have happened? Think about it. If they had held on to him and not let go, what would have happened? If they had been a nation that could unite with Jesus, Israel would not have perished. How miserable has the current Israel become? They are suffering immensely. The remnants of that tribe still exist because God protects them... and that is something to be grateful for.

God established Israel as a fence to find the son who could be the object of comfort amidst the realm of Satan, but they did not know that. If God had set that son as the object of comfort, what would He give to that son? Would He give him the world of Satan? No. The loving God intended to give Israel as a gift, which He had prepared for 4,000 years. It is a shocking fact.

Jesus is the object of God's comfort, the center of victory before all humanity. This Jesus is the son of God, bone of His bone, and the object of comfort who can communicate God's heart. What would He give as a gift upon that victorious foundation? Would He build brick houses? What would He give? Think about it. He wanted to give the world. How could He give the world? Even if He wanted to give heaven and earth, it cannot be done just by words. That is why a nation is needed. In other words, the nation of Israel was necessary.

What if Jesus had received the selected nation of Israel centered on the nation that was prepared for 4,000 years? You must understand this. Israel had this responsibility, yet they thought only about prospering their own nation. They believed they could be fine without the Messiah. When that happens, they are destined to perish.

God must have a being who can be the best of the best, who can proudly stand in the historical process. There must be one man, one son who can come forth. God, saying to Satan, "Hey, I have worked for thousands of years to establish such a son. You opposed it, but look today," must have a son who can truly say, "Yes, that is right. They are all my love." Such a son must exist.

By having that one son, God should be able to forget the world and be pleased. Only then can the world of Satan be forgotten. The joy felt by embracing that one person and seeking that one person must be so great that it can overshadow all the sorrows woven into the world of Satan. Such a being must come forth. Otherwise, it will not be possible to overcome the fallen state from Eden. In other words, it is impossible to establish a standard of emotional comfort in God's heart.

Such a person has been sought until now. But has that person come? They are coming. That is why the nation of Israel says the Messiah is coming, and today Christians say the Lord is coming. Then where will that person come to fulfill the mission of the Messiah? In which land will they be born? You must know this.

What you need to understand is that before meeting that person, you must first know the path God has taken to send Him. Only then can you be reborn directly through that person. In other words, God has been seeking the path of blessing from the family of Adam until now to send one Messiah to this earth. We must understand that for the purpose of eventually establishing an absolute son of God as the substantial object of love and comfort, God has walked for 6,000 years from the family of Adam until now.

There are no saints among women. Women may feel offended hearing this, but there are no saints. So when can women find dignity? When they meet that person (the Messiah) and become brides. That is why Christianity is called a bride religion.

The death of Jesus became an unspeakable sorrow for God. 

Then that son must carry out a pioneering history to give birth to humanity again. Until that son comes, who has been guiding? Who was guiding for the 4,000 years before Jesus came? God did it directly. Think about how much sorrow God must have endured to find that son. He had to create a person on God's side who was more loyal, filial, and virtuous than those in the enemy's nation. Moreover, it was not God who gave birth and raised him, but God had to take him from the world of Satan and make him a person on God's side, which must have caused God immense pain. It is a shocking matter. How easy would it have been for God to make Satan's offspring understand His circumstances and heart? It is not an easy task. The 4,000 years were rather quick for God. Until that son came, until Jesus was born in Bethlehem, God had to do that work.

Then how many times do you think God has traveled back and forth on this fallen earth? How many times do you think? Before Jacob went to Haran, before Abraham offered sacrifices, before the flood judgment of Noah, if you keep going back, you will come to Cain and Abel from the family of Adam. Did God not come there and say, "Abel, the law of heaven has been turned upside down, so please, please subdue Cain and restore it"? Did He pray that way or not? How much did God pray in His heart for Cain to be subdued? The heart that God earnestly desired is incomparable to the prayers of fallen humans today who long for God and want to understand God's heart. How earnestly must He have hoped? Think about God's earnestness as He looked upon Abel, who knew nothing and was inadequate, and staked everything on him.

It is shocking that the one who came with such earnest hope had to be chased away by Satan. Satan danced with joy, while God had to turn back down the path He had come with tears in His eyes. From there, miserable days of having to return began for God. You must understand that because He did not have the center of the foundation He desired, God came down to find one center amidst the history of the world and numerous nations.

You all say that Korea will become a beloved nation before God's will and can fulfill His purpose as the third Israel. Christianity is not originally a Western religion. Christianity should not be confined to the Middle East. It has been over 200 years since Christianity was spread to Korea after going around Europe. Did God only start coming about 200 years ago? Until Korea reached such a position, God developed history from the West while secretly preparing historical connections and circumstances from the East. Without that, His purpose could not be fulfilled. Furthermore, while encompassing numerous nations from behind the scenes, He has gone through trials and pains without caring about them to focus on one moment. You must think about how great God's efforts behind the scenes have been.

God established Noah in place of Abel after 1,600 years. Then He established Abraham, Moses, John the Baptist, and Jesus. However, until now, God has stood in a position of repeated failure. If He were a human, He would not be able to show His face with dignity. He would say, "I don't know. Let it be as it will." He would give up everything. But God could not do that.

Think about it quietly. Such humiliation and contempt, the ridicule and scorn of enemies, and not only that, the bloodshed and death were frequent, so think about God's heart that had to hold funerals every day. How many Christians were massacred during the time of the Daewongun? Whenever Christianity enters a country, Christians are martyred. In this way, God has endured the sorrow of daily defeats as His people, whom He raised with devotion, fell one after another. You must understand God's circumstances.

In such a situation where God has no comfortable days, today Christians say that God is in glory, so it is natural for God to groan over the creation of humanity, as it is written in the Bible. It is impossible not to groan. God can only groan... How did He become a God for whom groaning is natural?

A person, a group, a nation, a state is needed to bear the responsibility of repaying the enemies with the grievances and sorrows related to this. That one son must come and become the subject of God's comfort while also repaying this enemy. Because the sons and daughters fell, they must be restored as the objects of comfort.

That is why Jesus referred to Himself as the bridegroom and sought a true female entity who could become the bride, receiving God's love, but He could not fulfill His purpose and left with grievances. 

"Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will." In this prayer of Jesus lies the grief of 4,000 years of history. Moreover, knowing that many people in the future must cross the altar of blood in the historical process, He bore the shocking circumstances and appealed.

What about Peter, James, and the apostles? What makes them different from Peter and you? After all, they watched Jesus carry the cross and stayed quiet, and they ran away, so you are better than them. Still, because they repented after Jesus died and resurrected, they were given the name of apostles again. In other words, it was reversed. That is why Peter died upside down. You may feel uncomfortable, but you must know that the religion passed down from those apostles is Christianity. Do you believe in the religion established by those who betrayed Him? The Teacher protests against them. He attacks them. It is a shocking matter.

No matter how much you pray for blessings and seek a foundation of happiness, if the emotional object of comfort that God was seeking does not appear, those prayers cannot be fulfilled. If they are fulfilled, it will rather become a disaster. The blessing of Israel was to create a fence to receive the Messiah. Israel could have been lifted up as a glorious nation among all nations, but instead, it became a disaster. It would have been better if they had not been blessed.

Therefore, before God, who lost Adam, that is, because God lost the subject of comfort representing the men of this earth, the emotional object that can replace that subject must come forth again on this earth. Adam could have easily nestled in God's embrace, but because he was the cause of pain and sorrow, he must come again to comfort all the historical sorrows that God suffered in the past and to remove the grievances caused by humanity's fall from God's heart. After that, he must go beyond to the position of being able to comfort as the victorious son.

You must understand that God has paved the way for thousands and millions of times until Jesus comes in the position of such a son. God chose the nation of Israel as His chosen people to establish a son who could be the subject of comfort, and sent Jesus, hoping to lead all people to where God is, for 4,000 years. However, when Jesus carried the cross and wore a crown of thorns heading to Golgotha, do you think God's heart was pleased? It was shocking for Him. If Jesus came to die like that, why did God prepare for 4,000 years? The death of Jesus on the cross was purely due to the failure of the people of Israel to take responsibility. Do you not know that? Did Jesus die to save all people? If the dead Jesus saves all people, does that mean the living Jesus cannot save them?

To completely comfort God, you must understand that the being that should stand as the tangible entity of God has fallen, and that the history up to now has been the providence to restore that. If the Lord came alone and became the subject of comfort, what would happen next? 

"God, just look at me. Is it not enough for just me?" Would that be acceptable? The fallen motivation of humanity is because of Adam, and even if Jesus stands in the position of the son in place of Adam, there are still many people remaining in the world of Satan. It is not possible to abandon all humanity and judge them. Because Adam made a mistake, the son who comes to fulfill the responsibility in place of Adam must stand in the position to save all the people of this world. Jesus cannot serve God alone. He just went to the Garden of Gethsemane and prayed all night... Jesus could not even enter the position to comfort God, so how unjust must the sorrows He experienced on this earth have been?

At that time, the nation of Israel should have united as one centered around Jesus. To what extent should they have united? They should have united more than Jacob did when he wrestled with the angel at the Jabbok River. If Jesus crossed the sea, they should have crossed with Him; if He went up the mountain, they should have gone up with Him, and if the entire nation of Judah had followed and gathered around Jesus like a swarm of locusts, what would have happened? A new historical movement would have begun from there. Although God prepared for 4,000 years for that time, they lost all the prepared foundations. 

What did Jesus do when He came to this earth? He wept to resolve the grievances bound in history. He had to pray to fulfill the wishes of the ancestors who shed tears, asking for the Messiah to come at the end and resolve their frustrations and grievances. Because the tears shed by the ancestors were not collected, Jesus...
You are the Father, please take away their tears. This is what I had to pray.  
However, after praying, the nation should have welcomed joy, but despite Jesus praying and repenting on behalf of individuals and nations, there was total opposition. Again, disregarding God's dignity, I pleaded, "Father, please forgive," and after receiving forgiveness, when I stepped forward, there was more opposition. Thus, the way to forgive was blocked. Even after trying dozens of times, there was no possibility, and the price of that forgiveness was the path of the cross that Jesus walked with His life. It is a shocking story that the path Jesus walked was the path of the cross.  
Do you believe in Jesus and think you will go to heaven without knowing this? For example, when a woman gets older, she gets married. Anyone can get married. However, one can be kicked out of the in-laws' house, be mistreated by the husband, or live as a widow in the in-laws' house. How will you go to your in-laws? You want to get married in a place where everyone envies you, where everyone can fall in love with you, right? Is it easy to achieve that? Likewise, they say if you believe, you will go to heaven. But what kind of place is heaven? It is a place of utmost sincerity, a place of utmost loyalty, a place of utmost stories. What do you believe to go to such a place?  
Then how should you go believing? You must go to a place where blood and tears intersect. When Adam fell and was cast out, did he leave saying, "Ha ha, this is great!"? He left shedding blood and tears. To return to the house from which you were cast out, you must be better than Adam, right? For example, if you were cast out of the neighborhood and want to return, can you go back being worse than before? Therefore, you must be better than Adam. If you return from a place worse than Adam, you will surely be cast out again. God will rebuke you, saying, "You child!"  
Because God desires you to return from a place better than Adam, the Unification Church is conducting evangelism based on a seven-year standard. When you go out to evangelize, you may face persecution in that neighborhood, and some may have been beaten. And in the place of being cast out, there may be those who swore firmly to come back. Thus, when you return with qualifications and content that they never even dreamed of, you will stand in a place where you can resolve your grievances. From there, you can do as you wish. Something new will unfold. But if you cannot do that, you are just a disgrace. Is there no way?  
God, who has come out to gather the fallen behind the scenes,  
If a better place is not created than the place where Jesus died, you will be cast out again. That is why God hastened Christianity even if it meant crossing the threshold of death. He did not mind sacrificing one nation to find many nations. God, while longing for the day when He can wash away the shame of the returning sons at the end of days and create a situation and environment where He can appear with the attitude of a true son of God, has pushed and pushed, developing Christianity despite the sacrifices behind the scenes. You must understand this providence of God. Thus, the history of Christianity has been marked by the history of martyrdom. To resolve grievances and sorrows, heaven has worked to create a group that can stand between heaven and earth. Those who think that if they believe and remain still, our Lord will come to find them have ruined Christianity. Moreover, it would be better if they kept their mouths shut, but they claim to be orthodox.  
How can we comfort God? You must understand the historical story of how the central being of comfort will come to this earth. To establish him, God has worked behind the scenes to gather the defeated and the fallen countless times. You must understand God's heart in this. Those who think they are great have all been swept away by the world, but God has led those who were lost and wandering the path of death.  
Such people are those who can resonate with God's heart, and thus, the situation of gathering and restoring those fallen lives is truly astonishing. The young people, however, all say they dislike it, so throughout history, those called by God have all been over 50, over 60. They are people who are old and worn out, who will soon have to go to the grave, a group whose days of funeral songs are drawing near. Behind the scenes, God is currently working with this worn-out and dried-up elderly population, but in the future, He must work with the middle-aged. He has been concerned about how to develop providence while holding onto them. This is the story that has been carried through history.  
The era of old age must pass, and the era of middle age must come, the era of middle age must pass, and the era of youth must come, the era of youth must pass, and the era of boyhood must come, the era of boyhood must pass, and the era of infancy must come. Thus, you must be reborn. Otherwise, you cannot go to heaven. You must be able to be loved like an innocent child. That is why Jesus said to Nicodemus that he must be born again. He said that one must be reborn, that is, one must be born again. Therefore, God wants to carry out the work of salvation from the womb of the mother as the highest restorative history. What a remarkable story this is!  
Raise the young people.  
Today, the grandparents of the Unification Church must retreat. Does that make you feel bad? When I say to retreat, I am not blocking the way to heaven. Shouldn't the era pass for God to be comforted? Looking closely, there are many older people in the Unification Church, which is quite difficult. To achieve restoration and indemnity, one must be vigorous like the young people, but since they cannot do that, they are left with no choice but to rely on the teacher. How pitiful is it to be in such a situation? You must understand that. Until now, you have survived by relying on God, on Jesus, and on countless Christians, and now you are still relying on the young people of the Unification Church. It is a shocking matter. You must strive not to rely on others.  
Therefore, older people must serve God while shedding tears and making efforts. Elders, uncles, and aunts with families should lament, "Why couldn't I have sons and daughters who can replace God and the Messiah in my family?" While others have better sons and daughters who are loyal to God, why doesn't my family have such sons and daughters? They should feel ashamed when they see the mountains and rivers and feel unable to lift their faces when looking around. Since there are no such sons and daughters, they should at least go around the neighborhood and say they will resolve God's grievances and the grievances of a thousand years. They must realize that they are couples in the middle-aged group.  
However, you are eating as you please, wearing what you want, and doing whatever you want, and that becomes the condition for accusation.  
Oh, others' husbands earn money well, but look at me. Is it my responsibility to complain? Middle-aged couples should realize that they are ashamed before God because they do not have young people who can be loyal to God. They must raise such young people even now.  
Fortunately, there is a law in our Unification Church that there are children of faith. The children of faith can save middle-aged couples. For this, you must truly strive until your bones melt. When you shed tears of hope before the young people, the Messiah will come upon the foundation of that youthful hope. Will God work with old men like Peter or with leftover scraps? Think about it. Would God come to find someone like a leftover cucumber stem? Even flies do not land on a cucumber stem floating in lukewarm water... You must create connections that can resolve these grievances by guiding your sons, daughters, nephews, and cousins.  
Many spirits in the spirit world are longing for their descendants on earth to stand before the heavenly principles with the connections of indemnity. You must understand this will and strive to create connections that can take responsibility, even if you cannot fulfill all responsibilities.  
A person who can comfort God must come forth.  
The Lord who comes to this earth must be someone who can empathize with God's heart, which has been sorrowful at the sight of humanity created by love falling. Otherwise, you must understand that you cannot be a subject of comfort before God.  
That is why Jesus, carrying the cross with such a story, prayed to forgive their sins. And because He understood such a heart of Jesus, God could be with Him in that prayer.  
But is the standard you believe in a standard that can comfort God? God is pitiful. This is not just a saying; it is a fact. When you look at the condition of your heart and body, can you truly say that you are the son or daughter God is looking for?  
You cannot enter heaven without comforting God. But how can you comfort God? Are you going to eat whatever you want, wear whatever you want, do whatever you want, and then offer the leftovers as comfort? Absolutely not! Even Satan dislikes that. If you place a piece of bread in front of kindergarten students, they will not want it if it has dirt on the corner.  
If even the children of fallen humans feel that way, how would the Creator of heaven and earth feel? The more you think about it, the more you realize your own shortcomings, and as you go further, you realize how insufficient you are to forgive the grievances of a thousand years in your heart. When you think about how to escape from this environment that has made you feel like this, can you really say that you are not aware of your own situation?  
Who will comfort God's grievances? There must be sons and daughters who can comfort God centered on Jesus, a couple who can become one, and a loyal subject who can emerge. But who will do it? "Oh, we are too busy living our lives, so let Jesus do it alone." Such people are thieves. They are a burden to Jesus. These people are traitors.  
Because the heart of God, which has been tangled for 6,000 years, has been like this, the son whom God has sought must also be such a son. Knowing this, we strive not to become such sons but to do so, so hear this crying voice. Look upon this struggling situation.  
It must be possible. Without going through this process, it is impossible to comfort God.  
You must clearly understand that God is a God of sighs, unable to resolve the heart of sighing. We must become sons and daughters who can comfort God's heart and the story of His sighs. Who dares to look at the father who holds such sons and daughters in his arms? However, looking at such a God is the greatest hope of humanity, and achieving such a moment should be our goal.  
You must be able to assure yourself of this. Therefore, you must welcome that day. You must establish someone who can do so. That is, if someone is slightly better than you, you must establish them, and if someone works harder, you must establish them. You must have the heart to establish someone better than yourself. The Israelites, who failed to fulfill their responsibility to create a foundation that could welcome the coming Messiah at the center of the world, have perished. History has shown this.  
Therefore, with all your strength, embrace God and say, "Father, how did this happen? It is because our ancestors made mistakes. Are not these sons and daughters the ones you desired? Is not this family the family you envisioned?"  
You must understand that it is the responsibility of the Lord who is coming to resolve God's story. The Lord who is coming must do this. He must come for that responsibility. Adam and Eve, the substantial reality of comfort who left grievances before heaven and earth, must have established the standard of true ancestors of humanity who made mistakes. However, because this could not be achieved and grievances were left unresolved, Jesus and the Holy Spirit became sons and daughters, became husband and wife, and came carrying the mission of pioneering with tears of blood over 2,000 years of historical process. You must understand this.  
Jesus hoped to fulfill the mission of being both a son and daughter while also fulfilling the mission of being a couple. And He hoped for the position of a loyal subject. Jesus had to subdue all nations and present them before God, saying, "Please accept this." Thus, He had to fulfill the duty of filial piety and the duty of a loyal subject before God.  
What must the Messiah do? He must lay the foundation of a family-centered Messiah, establish the standard of a global family, and set the standard of a global loyal subject to build a new heaven and earth and establish the laws of the heavenly kingdom. This is the mission of the Lord. However, things like the sound of the archangel's trumpet and being lifted into the air are all just tricks for personal enjoyment.  
Humanity has not yet completed the standard of loyalty and filial piety on this earth. As true parents, standing in place of heaven and earth, men must represent heaven and women must represent earth, and by uniting as a true bride and groom, they can stand as subjects of comfort before God. This is established through the coming of the Lord. Thus, that family must become a loyal family, and a national standard of loyalty must be laid down so that all nations can follow. This is the standard that the coming Messiah must achieve. Therefore...
The Lord does not come in glory. The Lord carries a bundle of suffering that is inseparably attached to Him. 

Even if there are 3 billion people in the world, from God's perspective, there are only two: man and woman. That is why Jesus said to follow Him. Therefore, you must become sons who represent Jesus and daughters who represent the Holy Spirit, possessing the essence of the bridegroom and bride, and fulfill your wishes before God. You must be able to do this. In other words, you are being called to restore the qualifications of the Messiah as the bridegroom and bride, and the qualifications of a familial Savior. Until now, Jesus was the only Savior. In other words, women have not been given the qualifications to participate in the Messiah until now.

By establishing the duty of loyalty from the family, when this becomes the center of all nations, the ideal of the Messiah will be realized. When the Messiah stands on the earth and fulfills His responsibilities, and when this world is offered to God, the mission of the Messiah will be concluded. Only then can we finally transcend this fallen world.

When have you ever wept all night to comfort God? 

The Messiah who is coming now is pitiful. Of course, you are pitiful too, but what does it matter if you are pitiful a hundred or a thousand times? That pitiful being was born ugly. However, what does the cross mean for Jesus, who came after 4,000 years of preparation? It is not God's will for the Son of God to bear the cross; it is not Jesus' wish. If you understood this, then on the path of faith, where there is a valley of death, you must have the heart to go first and fill that valley. Do the members of the Unification Church do this today? They are good at observing and following, but they are quick to calculate, saying, "Oh no, if it’s going to be a loss, I shouldn’t do it." However, God has been full of losses until now. He has been the king of losses, establishing a kingdom of losses.

Now, let us comfort God! We are to comfort Him as sons. We must dedicate our bodies and work as sons. When have you ever wept and struck the ground all night for your own life and problems? If you cannot do that for your own life, what hesitation is there in doing God's work? Have the women fully played their roles as daughters of God? There are women like Yu Gwan-sun in South Korea, but if you were told to die for a cause, you would all run away. The fierce world of enemies stands before us and does not retreat easily. It will not retreat by hesitating, so unless we push forward, we cannot resolve it. This is the state of fallen humanity.

Then, what is one of the three great wishes of fallen humanity? The completion of the restoration of individuality, meaning I must complete it. To complete it, we must settle the emotional debts we owe to God. Therefore, we must bear the cross. The sins of Israel can only be forgiven through the process of sacrifice, so we must pay the price of blood. Without paying that price, whether it be tears or sweat, there can be no atonement. That is why Jesus said to pray without ceasing.

When you pray, do you pray comfortably, spreading your arms and lying down? You must kneel, strike your forehead against the stone, and pray even if your nose bleeds. If comfort were the way, then the founder of the Unification Church would have already been the last. It is good that it is not comfortable. It is because it has not been comfortable that we have come this far. You must understand that. It cannot be done in a comfortable place.

So even now, if you think back to the past, what do you miss the most? The times when you ate well and played well are not remembered by the teacher. No matter how well you ate, once your stomach is full, it becomes a burden. You had to eat, but you ate with the mindset of incurring a debt. The most memorable times are when I was chased, pursued, captured, tortured, and coughed up blood. Those moments remain the most vivid in my memory. Remembering that place, when I say, "Father!" I can feel God's heart turning upside down and His clothes being turned inside out, but memories of eating well and living well are ultimately unnecessary. The hardships of youth are worth more than gold. And even amidst suffering, you must be able to endure.

Let me tell you a story from when I was in Hungnam prison. At that time, I worked at the Hungnam fertilizer factory, tying fertilizer bags. The hardest job was tying the fertilizer bags with string. In winter, if you used string, clothes made of cotton would fall apart in less than three days. You had to tie 1,300 bags a day, and ten people had to do this in eight hours. If the daily quota was 130 bags per person, that is heavy labor. A regular person cannot do 75 or 80 bags, but they were told to do it by the ship's standard, which is like telling them to die. The communists were making us do such work.

You must understand what the communists are like. I am not a supporter of the ruling party, but these days, the opposition party in South Korea is rampaging without knowing the world. Even if we are wearing rags, we must sell all our possessions for three years or five years to save the country. They do not realize that the end is coming. Those who do not know the world are the first to run away when problems arise. We cannot trust such people. You must understand that.

In the prison where I was, there was a strong ammonia smell from the urine, and if it got on your clothes, the smell was terrible, but more than the smell, the clothes would develop holes in just one day. It was a brutal job to the point where the fabric would tear. When holes appeared, you had to mend them, but can you mend them with your fingers? 

What do you miss the most in that place? Of course, it is food. When someone came to visit, you would miss the story, but more than the person's face, you would look at their hands. Those who have been in the military will understand this feeling a bit. When someone comes to visit, it is not about what they are wearing but what they have brought. Those who have not experienced it will not understand. When you fast for a week, what is the feeling ten minutes before midnight on the seventh day? When you see death in that moment, you would be happier than anything else in the world. How desperate is that?

Food is what you miss the most, but next, what do you miss? A needle. Even if you want to sew your clothes, do you have a needle or thread? There is nothing, so those who have spent a long time in prison become scavengers. If you find a piece of cloth on the ground, you pick it up, no matter if it has dung on it. Talking about shame or pride is useless. I said goodbye to shame long ago; where is the shame? It is rather a point of pride. Do you understand that feeling? If you look at the belongings of those who have spent more than five or ten years in prison, you will see that they have all sorts of things. They may not be big, but they have their necessities.

If there is a needle anywhere, you negotiate for it. So, even if you get one, you have to pay a bribe to use it. If you do not know someone, they will not lend it to you. So when a needle appears in a cell, it becomes a hot commodity. Whether it was borrowed from someone close or brought by a new arrival, chaos ensues. If I say I am the elder, I rush in, and the person who borrowed it cannot sew but just watches, and when the owner asks for it back, they must return it. At that time, I thought to myself, where else could I find something of such value as a needle?

Whenever I see my split teeth in the mirror, I remember something. I used to sew bags with thin wire, and there is a tool to insert that wire. It is made of steel. To make a needle, you would place it on the rail and tap it until it flattens. However, even if it flattens, it cannot pierce a hole, so it had to be bent to be made. You had to bend it well; if you bent it wrong and it broke, it would mean ten years of study wasted. So I tried this and that until I finally made it. It was truly difficult. Those who have not experienced such things cannot understand. You cannot know just by hearing about it. There are glass windows high up in the factory. When you need glass, you just break the window. This is not something I did; other people did such things. (Laughter) Whether the guards are there or not… The guards cannot help it. Since they cannot do it, it cannot be helped. So, you get a piece of glass and try to sew the bag, but can you match the holes? You have no choice but to unfold the fertilizer bag and re-pierce the holes, but the wire gets bent in the middle, and it breaks with a third left. You have no choice but to choose a sturdier wire, but as you try to use it, it keeps getting tangled. So I bit the wire with my teeth to cut it, and that is how I split my teeth. It is an unforgettable souvenir. Every time I see my teeth, I think of that time. But is sewing a problem today? To the ladies of the Unification Church, from now on, you should say, "Has the needle come?" (Laughter) "What a precious thread it is."

As I continued working, one day after a year and a half, while I was sewing a bag, I found a needle in that bag. The bags were all brought from the countryside, and it seems that a needle had fallen in while they were gathering them. So I got one needle. The news spread among the 800 to 1,000 inmates in the prison, "Hey, someone found a needle!" When I found that needle, I was as happy as if I had received a revelation from God. Everyone there knows how to do anything. I can even make underwear. The cloth used to wrap books in school was good for making underwear. (Laughter) I can knit. I can do anything without relying on women; I can live splendidly on my own.

To comfort God, you must be in the same situation. 

You who believe in Jesus must think, "I am the representative of Jesus." And even if you are in Cain's position, try to imitate the tears Jesus shed for the nation. If you try to imitate, the imitation will become real. Otherwise, you will not understand Jesus' heart.

You cannot understand the heart of the hungry without being hungry yourself. You cannot know unless you have been in the same position. If you want to know what the Messiah's situation is like, you must stand in the same position as the Messiah. If you are the Holy Spirit, you must stand in the position of the Holy Spirit. If you are God, you must stand in God's position; otherwise, you will not know that situation. So how can you stand in such a position? The principles of the Unification Church teach you that method.

You must comfort God. How can you go to heaven without comforting God and settling the debts that humanity has incurred by betraying Him? If you say you will go to heaven without settling your sins, that is no different from the mindset of a thief.

Therefore, just as Jesus was chased and persecuted, you too must experience being chased and persecuted. You must be used by bad people and be chased for the sake of the nation, the people, and the world, from a public standpoint. Even when you are chased, do not be sorrowful.

When April passes, pray and reflect on your entire life up to now. April is always a time of overcoming a hurdle. When you reflect on the past, there will be countless events. You will feel that you are walking the path of restoration while being chased and pursued. When you are persecuted, has God said, "You deserve to be treated that way"? Or have you lived in a way that when you are in such a position, God can be with you, weeping when you weep, and grieving when you grieve? If you have not lived such a life, you must repent.

The purpose of entering the Unification Church and learning the principles is to comfort God. So how do you comfort God? You must be prepared to die to take responsibility for the lives of the 30 million people of South Korea. You must pray for the 30 million people of South Korea day and night. You must put forth all your efforts to drive out the evildoers who block the work of saving the nation and paving the way for goodness. Furthermore, Unification Church members must take responsibility for the world. Since Jesus could not take responsibility, we must try to take responsibility. We must fight against the communists who deny God. Even if we fall on the front lines against the communists and their guns, we must fight. That is why I have been traveling abroad for the past four or five years, but thinking of them makes me feel bad, so I cannot go around. The enemies within the country are not the problem. We must recognize that the enemies outside the country are lurking.

In such an environment, what will the Unification Church do? We must establish the connection and heart of God that this nation has not had among its people, and we must establish the heavenly connection that the world has not thought of on this earth. When that happens, the work you do itself will be able to comfort God.

Three Judgments at the End

To conclude, we are in debt. Humanity, created by God's word, has not fulfilled the fruits of that word. Therefore, you must set the standard that Adam should be like this, and a perfected person should be like that according to the principles. To fulfill the fruits of the word, you must become the reality, and that reality must fight against Satan and win, establishing a loving relationship with God.

That is why, at the end, there will be the judgment of truth and the judgment of heart. To become the reality of comfort that comforts God, you must fulfill all the conditions of such judgment. When Jesus came to this earth and said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life. No one comes to the Father except through me" (John 14:6), what does this mean? It means that He is the Jesus of truth and the Jesus of life; truth is the word, and life refers to the reality. After that comes love.

"I am the way, the truth, and the life…" There is no mention of God's love here. In other words, if He had said, "I am the way, the truth, the life, and love; no one comes to the Father except through me," then everything would have been included.

Until now, the countries that boast of being advanced nations by creating a cultural world in the 20th century say they have no philosophy or ideology to emulate. Therefore, they are in a position to revolutionize with God's truth. The ideology of communism is also not a truth that can please God. Looking at today's society, can we say, "The words of one truth are connected to daily life, and daily life is lived with the truth I hoped for. The foundation of the relationship I desired has become a relationship of truth"?
When I asked what it was, they mumbled that it was a difficult yet easy question. However, when I ask you, "What is God's will? What is the true path of life?" you will respond with, "This is how it is." This is where you differ from them. You must have a purpose in your journey, but today’s human world does not. The providence regarding America and Korea
As I traveled through the 48 states of America, just looking at the roads, I could tell it was a wealthy country. Among the places I visited, the border area between Arizona, Nevada, and California is mountainous, with the Grand Canyon and rivers flowing through it. This has been happening since the earth was formed thousands of years ago; when it rains, the rainwater gathers in one place and begins to flow as a river. Thus, this valley was formed, and later the mountain range was cut off from the river. The width of this river is about 150 to 200 meters, and the valley through which the water flows is all made of blue stone, but now this river has been dammed to create a dam for power generation. This dam is the Hoover Dam. The height of this dam is 172 meters. The construction cost of this dam was about 300 million dollars. It is known as a global construction project in the late 20th century.

So I checked how much cement was used for that dam. The road from San Francisco to Washington is a journey that takes a week, driving 6 hours a day at 100 miles per hour, and this road is entirely paved with cement. It is said that the amount of cement used to build this road was equivalent to that used for the dam.

In any case, America is a large country. But why is Korea so small…. My ambition is greater than that of America, so why was I born in such a small Korea? My ancestors lived here too. Anyway, in America, I couldn’t find any crooked roads. They were all straight and well-paved. If you just hold the steering wheel, you can drive smoothly, but in Korea, every road is winding and crooked, making it hard for drivers.

Looking at Korea today, they say it’s a beautiful land, but if you go to a scenic spot and venture a little further back, the smell is so bad that you can’t help but cover your nose.

However, America’s scenic spots are clean everywhere, allowing you to park your car and enjoy the view pleasantly. Even the grass is all golden grass, and when you get out of the car and walk through such soft places, it feels really good. Just looking at it makes you feel good. After driving more than a hundred miles a day, your back starts to hurt. At that time, if you get out of the car and rest on the grass, it feels really good. Such experiences cannot be found anywhere other than in America. Also, the roads are paved so beautifully.

In Korea, because the land is small, even when building factories, they build them high. Of course, there are some factories in America with huge smokestacks. However, most factories are single-story; two or three-story factories are rare. And when they face technical difficulties, they make sure to research that field and inform people about it.

It is certain that Johnson, the president of America, is a descendant of fallen ancestors. All descendants born of fallen ancestors are fake. They must bow their heads before the true. If the poorest laborer from a slum in Korea knows and serves his true parents before President Johnson, who will be the elder brother among them? If a child runs to the true parents, saying, "Aren't you my mother and father?" then the true parents cannot abandon him. If he enters a place where he has met his true parents before President Johnson, it doesn’t matter whether he lives in a tent or any house. Even if he sleeps in the most miserable place, he will eventually become the elder brother of those who live luxuriously in America. The Korean people have met their true parents first, so they become the elder brothers. Do you all understand this now? "Yes."

The age of persecution has passed, but we do not feel it, and we believe. From a providential perspective, as the benefits of the times approach us, the issues of struggle do not diminish; rather, they become even greater. Therefore, the environment we face has a great enemy entrenched, and God must also prepare for this, working in such a way that I can surpass the opposing side centered on me. Thus, everything felt at that time has become an essential resource that cannot be excluded from our current perception.

After such external opposition has passed, I find myself in a position where I am ultimately alone, standing in a place without enemies. Can being in such a position serve as a stepping stone for God to cooperate? Absolutely not. God has worked at times when it is possible to attack the world of the enemy, at moments when a final decision can be made. He cannot work during ordinary times.

We currently do not have the environmental conditions to approach God, pledge our loyalty, and repel evil. This is the focal point of the issue that you must understand.

In the past, during difficult times, we always felt the presence of heaven and Satan. We clearly realized that we were standing on the boundary between heaven and Satan. However, now that external persecution has disappeared, our perception of the sides of Satan and heaven has changed. Because of this, even when praying centered on the purpose, it does not feel real, and even when going out to evangelize, it does not feel real. God has worked in a way that doubles the power of two over one, allowing us to advance toward tomorrow with that strong force. However, today you have lost the necessity of comrades.

The world today is a result of the consequences of the Fall.
In the world, there is a saying that if you plant beans, you will harvest beans, and if you plant red beans, you will harvest red beans. This means you reap what you sow. Today, the world is divided into two camps. Democracy and communism are in confrontation; one is based on idealism, and the other on materialism. This world has become one where these two ideologies are in opposition. Additionally, the youth issue has emerged as a global problem on this world stage.

So how did we arrive at this world of consequences? To put it simply, it is because we have sown in such a way that these results have appeared globally. We are witnessing the emergence of such a world.

People in today's world are all living in such an environment and are grappling with the huge problem of how to change such an environment. Those living in such times, especially those with religion, are saying that this is the end time. They are saying it is the end time. So what does the end time mean? It is the time when everything reaches its conclusion. The plants and grains that were revived in spring are harvested in autumn, marking the end time. From this perspective, we can think of this time as a historical harvest time, that is, the autumn season.

Humanity must inevitably settle the consequences of the Fall that were established when Adam and Eve fell. So what happened to the ancestors of humanity? Because they fell from a position not permitted by God, the body and mind that were to become one were divided like stone. In other words, one person became two. It is because they were sown in such a way that they have come through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, and now the time has come for this to bear fruit globally, which is the end time, or the last days.

Since humanity's ancestors were individuals who reproduced from the standpoint of a divided body and mind, they must inevitably bear fruit in the form of a divided body and mind. In other words, they cannot help but bear fruit as two worlds of idealism and materialism.

Thus far, we humans have lived while centering on our own minds and bodies, going through the process of struggle. We have not been able to run toward a clear purpose that follows the heavenly principles, achieving peace and unification on any given day. In other words, because the body and mind have fought, history has been sustained until now, and as a result, we could not help but be divided into these two worlds.

When we look at our body and mind, the mind always tries to move forward centered on one standard and one purpose, but the body always opposes that mind. The body has struck out against the mind. We know the historical fact that the external position has controlled, hindered, and attacked the internal position. Because we ourselves are like this, good and evil exist in a relative relationship, and among them, good is internal and evil is external, which is why the external evil has always attacked the internal good. This is the world of consequences that we are facing today. This is nothing more than the form of the struggle of our individual minds and bodies being expanded to a national, state, or global level.

Why must the end time come?
Then, will this form continue indefinitely to sustain history? It cannot. The wider the gap between our minds and bodies, the greater the suffering becomes. There is pain involved. Therefore, the issue lies within myself. I must resolve my own fundamental problems. Only on such a foundation can I connect with the world, and only then can a truly free and happy heaven be established. No matter how well the environment is prepared, if I am in a position where my own problems are unresolved, I cannot enjoy any happy environment.

Today, the world is in such a situation, which is a result of the Fall. In other words, the world today is a reflection of the struggle of my individual self projected globally. Originally, God did not create the world for humans to begin in struggle and end in struggle from such divided positions.

If humans had been centered on God, they could have united their bodies and minds forever. Therefore, the body and mind of humanity should have started as one on this earth. They should have been planted on this earth based on the standard of their unity.

In other words, we cannot deny the fact that this world has become what it is as a retribution for the Fall.

In other words, there is pain dwelling in my individual self that is struggling, and that pain inevitably becomes the basis for evil, so this must be resolved. If democracy had not emerged, what would the path of the Unification Church have been? To become the workers of harvest who fulfill the promise that God, who has sown goodness, will reap, we must seek out miserable places. Even from the peak of the cross, we must pass through the valley of death and declare that we will reap the fruits of goodness sown there, comforting God. In such places, we must think of God, who sets the goal of judging the world of death on this earth while we enter the place where He is saddened, saying, "I will gather the harvest you wish to reap."

The place where Jesus died was such a place, and the places where our ancestors, like Abraham, walked were also all such miserable places. Therefore, we must enter such places to gather our ancestors as the reality of resurrection and to possess the authority to comfort God's internal heart, so that we can fulfill our mission as workers of harvest.

To reap the fruits of goodness

God did not sow the seeds of goodness as a pastime or hobby. He sowed them with all His heart, with body and mind, with every cell and everything in His body united as one. Since it has been sown through trembling hands throughout history, those who have come forth to reap must also unite their body and mind, and in a place where their hearts cry out, their hands tremble, and all their nerves are concentrated, they must reap. In other words, since it was sown with all sincerity, they must reap with that same sincerity. Without becoming such a person, one cannot reap the fruits of goodness sown on this earth.

Therefore, we must go with tears. We must sow for humanity with our tears, for the earth with our sweat, and for heaven with our blood. Because God has gone through such a process, we can only feel God's heart in such places, and we can only reap what has been realized in those places. That is why the Unification Church teaches the way of heart. We must cultivate a personality that can communicate with the heart. Based on that standard, we should love our nation, and based on that standard, we should love the world. Thus, we must equip ourselves with the leading authority that can embrace and conquer this evil world, in other words, the authority that can conquer even the external world. Ultimately, we must unify the body and mind that humanity was originally meant to achieve, and based on that, we must realize a global fruit that can start a new world on this earth. This is the standard that the unification ideology must accomplish.

Since we are moving forward centered on such content, there must be misery in that process. Do you understand? "Yes." Tears must come to your eyes. You must shed blood and sweat as you walk this path. You must qualify to be an offering before heaven, thinking of the reality that you must go to the foundation where Christians fell miserably during the Roman Empire or under the tyranny of the righteous, and you must go out with the internal determination to become the reality of victory in such places. If such a scene exists today, you must become someone who swears before God to be the one running at the forefront.

To reap the fruits of goodness, we must go through the back alleys of the nation. Today, we must establish a standard to discern good and evil centered on the heavenly way, and that goodness lies in the back alleys of the evil world. It is in the back alleys! God is present in that world where miserable tears abound. Today, our Unification Church is walking that path. Is that good or bad? Without reaping the fruits of goodness sown in the tidal flats, we cannot eradicate evil. The Unification Church is destined to exist for that purpose.

Having returned victorious from the seven-year course, the teacher shed many tears of blood during those seven years. I don't know how you felt, but the teacher shed many tears of blood. Day and night, no matter how difficult the task, I ran around to achieve this one purpose. It is not something to blame others for not coming, nor is it something to blame for having no friends. I go because I have a mission to fulfill the results of God's predetermined providence. Thus, I must gather the fruits of goodness scattered throughout this world.

We must gather these fruits and unify ourselves, which have been divided through the scythe of the heart, and we must unify the separated heaven and human heart. This is the mission of those who are following the Unification Church today. Our bodies may be like dull scythe blades, but they must become the reality of tools used for harvesting. Through our reality, we must lead the world that is collapsing today correctly, and we must cross over to a new central world centered on God's heart. This is the mission of Unification Church members.

We must cut away the decadent trends of youth. With an authority that cannot be measured by anything, we must block and eliminate such worldly trends, severing all connections to the world of death led by Satan, and we must prevent the forces of death. It is our mission. As Unification warriors, we must fulfill these responsibilities and missions not individually but globally, centered on the heavenly earth. Only then will this heaven and earth be gathered as a completed fruit before God.

Knowing that we have such a mission, we must understand that the prayer we offered during the hundred-day prayer was to solidify our own position in fulfilling that mission. I hope you will put even more sincerity into starting the second seven-year course meaningfully. Thus, I hope you will become the workers of harvest who reap the fruits of goodness, remembered in heaven, and inherit the heavenly legacy. I say this with that meaning. Do you understand? "Yes."

We know that heaven's time has reached a certain standard. Now, let us tidy our expressions and postures, calling upon the Father in the clear blue sky, and let us run and dance, proclaiming that our time has come, in a world of freedom before us.
think about the approaching moment, and when I think that the sorrowful past can transform into joy, and that the unjust and heartbreaking facts can change into a time where they can boast of the glorious authority of the heavens, I realize that all of this, everything that has driven us into such a position, is the love of the Father who wishes to inherit Your heart. When I think of this, I can only offer my gratitude in countless ways. Let us stand on the side of Heaven. 
Matthew 27:27-31

<Words> We know well that the world we live in today is not on the side of Heaven. It is often the case that we cannot find anything on the side of Heaven, both in the world and in our personal lives. 

Fallen humanity must return to the side of Heaven. 

We have experienced many times in our lives that the struggle between conscience and body repeats infinitely. However, no matter how difficult, miserable, and chaotic our environment may be, we must seek the side of Heaven. This is a natural logic. It is also an undeniable fact that we must take this as our purpose and strive to achieve it desperately. 

In the position we are currently in, no matter how much we think, we cannot conceive of the side of Heaven. This is because everything we see is merely phenomena that oppose the side of Heaven, and our living environment is entangled with matters unrelated to the side of Heaven. When we think of this, we realize that seeking the side of Heaven and standing on the side of Heaven is exceedingly difficult. 

We must restore ourselves, standing at the crossroads of Heaven and Earth, God and Satan, good and evil, centering on goodness, and we must return to the side of God. We know well that this is the state of fallen humanity. That is why, until now, countless humans have sought God under the name of religion. We understand this fact well. 

Throughout the long course of history, many people have repeated such actions. We must recognize that we are in a fate where we cannot abandon this struggle while we are caught in it, and where we must continue to repeat it. 

In this way, we humans find ourselves in a very pitiful and miserable position, unable to assert ourselves before anyone.
We must understand this.
Up until now, we know well that no hero or martyr on this earth has ever dedicated their achievements, which they accomplished through various efforts to fulfill their inner resolutions, to God as something from the heavenly side. Countless humans have repeatedly harbored desires, but we also know the historical fact that they ultimately vanished along with their lamentations. However, in this environment, we must once again struggle and strive to break through this situation. This is our mission and our responsibility.
So what is the issue here? To stand on the side of heaven, we cannot stand on the side of humanity. In other words, human circumstances cannot connect with God's circumstances, human relationships cannot link to God's relationships, and human purposes cannot establish a relationship with God's purpose.
Therefore, in order to stand on the side of heaven, we must first think of God's will, live centered on God's will, and adopt a position of fighting with the goal of fulfilling God's will. God is one who connects through public paths, so He cannot come to places centered on private matters.
God can manifest His presence when standing on a greater public position through public standards. Only then can one draw closer to God. For this reason, many saints and sages have emphasized and taught the importance of a public stance.
What is the public position where God can manifest His presence?
From this perspective, what is the public position where God can manifest His presence? When we consider our human body and mind, the mind holds a more public position than the body. And if both body and mind have become my own in a public stance, we must stand on an even greater public position, which is the family. However, if the family is in a position contrary to my mind, establishing a public stance there becomes extremely difficult.
However, if there is a family that has established a public foundation, that family must stand on a public foundation centered on the nation. If a nation stands on a public foundation centered on the nation, that nation must stand on a global public foundation beyond the state. We know that we are destined to establish such a greater foundation, as this is the fate of fallen humanity.
Therefore, the path we must take does not end with living centered on my own conscience. It is essential to live while governing the body with conscience, to establish a good family, and even if a good family is established, to lead that family to form a good lineage, to lead that good lineage to form a good nation, and further to lead to a good state, a good world, and a good cosmos. This is the content connected to the path we are to take. Today, humanity does not realize how difficult this path is. Many people think that living centered on themselves, in whatever way, is the purpose of life.
In this environment, we are fighting to establish a public standard aimed at seeking the realm of God. That path, from a human perspective, can only be seen as infinitely miserable. The standard is not one that the whole can compromise on; it is an absolute standard that must deny the whole and step on it. We must understand that such an absolute standard is accompanied by misery.
While this public path is connected to humanity, God does not demand that only humans pave this path. Of course, it is true that humans are entrusted with this lonely and miserable position, but the entire responsibility is not placed solely on humanity. God is walking this path ahead of us, working hard behind the scenes to fulfill His own responsibilities. Many people living on this earth today are unaware of this fact.
When there is a true person, people may evaluate that person as true based on their outward actions, but they do not realize that the person has gone through countless struggles and faced numerous adversities to reach that position of truth, making resolutions and oaths without yielding. However, you must understand this fact well.
If this is true for one person, it is even more so for God, who sought to establish the heavenly side through the public historical path. We have lived until now without knowing that the greater God's desire for us to walk the public path, the more effort He has put in behind the scenes that humans do not know about.
In the process of pursuing goodness, if humans become even slightly disheartened or find themselves in a precarious position, they often embrace themselves and easily fall into despair. However, if one firmly understands that God is working hard for them in such a position, and that He is paving the way for them in even more miserable circumstances, then no matter how lonely and difficult the situation may be, they cannot succumb to despair. When comparing God and oneself, one can see that God stands in a cosmic position while they stand in a personal position. Furthermore, if one realizes that God's efforts are so great that they cannot be compared to their own, they can resolve to overcome all difficulties and follow God. This can also be understood through the common experiences of human society.
Today, humanity does not know whether God exists or not. If they knew that God exists, they should not forget that He is still enduring great suffering to pave the way for them, walking the public path while risking loneliness amidst numerous trials. This is true not only for non-believers but also for those who call God their Father and pursue the heavenly homeland in faith today. How many times have they forgotten that God has carried such an immense public historical path, only to stumble over their own grievances and curse God, betraying Him? How many historical facts of this nature have there been that we, as members of the Unification Church, are aware of?
So what should Unification Church members understand? They must first recognize the heavenly side that bears the responsibility in the public path more than anyone else.
God, who has faced difficulties greater than my own circumstances, who has faced difficulties greater than the circumstances of our nation, and who is bearing responsibility in an environment more difficult than the chaotic world today. If there are true children of God who genuinely care for such a God, He will undoubtedly seek them out more than anyone else.
Understanding God's misery
If there are people who know God, He will want to resolve the sorrows of history through them, impart the mission of the times, and entrust them with future responsibilities. Today, members of the Unification Church must be the first to stand at the forefront, recognizing the God who is in such sorrow, the God who is in such difficulty, and the God who is in such an unjust and indignant position.
When does the sorrow and injustice of humanity occur? It happens when the things I believed in and hoped for are shattered, or when the blood relationship I have with someone is denied. We know that this is the most miserable and painful time.
When a parent loves their child and believes in them, but that child betrays them, the shock, hardship, and misery the parent experiences is beyond words. Similarly, when someone who has risked their life to love another betrays and rejects them, it is also indescribably miserable. The pain of struggling in such a position is something that those who have not experienced it cannot understand. Words alone cannot convey this. This can be understood by reflecting on worldly matters.
So how did God become miserable? We must think about this once more. God is not an abstract being but a concrete one. He is also the one who has the highest relationship with humanity. If there is anything that can bring joy to God, it is seeing a starting point from which humanity can joyfully embark and continue toward the endless eternity. However, He lost that starting point because of humanity.
The place where God and humanity can rejoice together and sing of happiness is the place where God is not lost, where God is welcomed. In such a place, humanity was meant to be connected to God as children, but due to the Fall, all these connections were severed. From this perspective, humanity is the one who has driven God into a miserable position today. Until now, humanity has not realized this.
We have thought that God grieves in a position unrelated to us and that He labors from the perspective of a third party.
