We have not fully understood that all labor, pain, and sorrow are due to humanity, and that it is because of me, who represents humanity. In other words, we did not realize that God stands in such a position because of me. Knowing how miserable God was in the past and how miserable He is today, and understanding that He faced such despair for my sake, if there is someone who truly cares for such a God, that person cannot help but return to the side of heaven.
Thus, the question arises: where is the 'me' who has realized that I have such a connection with God?
God created all things and placed the human ancestors as the protagonists of all creation in the Garden of Eden. When creating humanity, He did not create them as a mere plaything or for amusement. The effort and sincerity God poured into creating humanity, to establish them as the center representing all things, is beyond description.
What kind of being was humanity created to be?
When God created humanity, He poured all His effort and devotion, as well as the essence of His life, into their creation, showering them with love and affection. Humanity was created in such a way that they cannot be separated by any force, nor can they be divided. Because humanity was created in this way, God can finally find peace in gazing upon them, and all affection and happiness can only dwell through humanity.
God is the Father of humanity, and humanity is the sons and daughters of God. Because humanity was created from God's bones, flesh, and marrow, they cannot draw God to themselves, nor can God draw them to Himself.
God created humanity in such a way that their content and purpose can align. If there were any words or poems that God could praise humanity with, it would be the highest work that no poet or writer in the world could express. The subject of such praise is neither God nor all things, but only humanity, which represents all things.
No matter how ugly or unattractive a person may appear, God's love can overflow through that person, God's words of life can sprout, and God's songs of love can be sung. Humanity, as fallen beings, possesses a level of dignity and high value centered on God that they cannot even dream of. We must recognize this fact. While this appearance may be that of an individual, God cannot help but see them as a representative of the universe. Why? Because He created humanity with all His focus and effort.
All things created around humanity served as stimulating symbols for them. The sound of birds could resonate with Adam's heart, serving as a motivation. Butterflies, bees, and all other creatures were created as symbolic and stimulating representations that Adam and Eve could not help but love. The blowing wind, flowing water, and even a single blade of grass in the field were all created as representations of the reality that loved Adam and Eve. Humanity was placed at the center of all creation. How blessed is this position of humanity? In God's eyes, humanity was a beloved creation, the ancestors of humanity whom He wished to embrace forever and never let go.
Holding onto Adam's hand, God said, "Adam, you and I have a bond that no one can ever sever." He was a Father who longed for a moment to make new plans and new promises.
Humanity, created in the eternal and unchanging bond of love, can become the center and core of peace. They must have the confidence to embrace and love all things in the universe. The Father and His sons and daughters, hand in hand, with hearts filled with emotion, saying, "Adam! Yes, Father!"—how much did God long for a moment to inherit all the works of heaven and earth and to be able to receive them? This was God's desire. However, on that day of desire, humanity fell without fulfilling the day that God had longed for. In other words, Adam and Eve, who longed for such a loving embrace, fell and died. The entirety of God's love and joy, represented by Adam and Eve, fell into the realm of death due to the Fall. They died.
Until now, God has stood in a position where He must turn to curses upon seeing His beloved children die, having lost His beloved children. God, who was in a miserable position where humanity, who was meant to be connected through the bond of love, suddenly appeared as a condition of curse, must have looked upon humanity, who could no longer call their sons and daughters as such. We must understand that the Fall of humanity was what brought God into such a miserable state.
The heart of a parent
Today, no matter how any writer tries to express it, the high-level love and value that has been distorted due to the Fall cannot be expressed. However, the one who witnessed humanity's Fall is none other than God, who stands in the position of a Father.
Parents who have given birth and raised children understand. They want to receive blessings and feel happiness through their beloved sons and daughters. They would also want to leave behind a standard of joy and blessings for their children forever if they could. With such hopes, even fallen humanity desires to be those sons and daughters. Day and night, they wish for their children to grow well, to be honored by all nations, and to be praised throughout the ages, wanting to protect them from harm and suffering.
The anxious heart of a parent is one that is open and vulnerable. This is also true for fallen parents. The earnest heart of a mother who raises her child while nursing them, even if the child soils themselves and smells bad, is a heart that can forget that environment through love. The heart of a fallen parent thinking about their child is the same, and how much more so the heart of God, the subject of love, who wanted to love Adam and Eve through His original heart? Everyone, think about this for a moment.

When you hold and raise a baby, singing songs to them while they sleep and talking to them in whispers, wishing for their well-being, this is a sentiment that any parent would have. No matter how flawed or lacking a child may be, if there is a defect in that child, the parent's heart experiences the utmost pain, and when that pain is resolved, the joy that accompanies it is proportional to that suffering. If the heart of a fallen parent is like this, how much more so is the heart of God?

As you know through the Principle, God loves humanity with a love that can make the whole world submit, granting authority that the entire universe can follow, and giving authority that can make the whole universe bow down completely. This is the highest love and the highest authority, which is why He entrusted responsibility to humanity.

Then why did God establish a division of responsibilities in human life? Being omniscient and omnipotent, He had to bestow that omniscient and omnipotent creativity, and being the eternal and unchanging subject of love, He could not help but give responsibilities to those who could represent that subject of love. This is a condition for blessing and is like a key that can conquer the whole. Therefore, He could not withhold this. However, we must understand that this division of responsibilities became a problem and led to the Fall.

You should not stand in the position of a third party. You are in a relationship with God regarding the division of responsibilities. When you were in the process of ascending to fulfill that division of responsibilities, how do you think God's heart felt when you attempted to violate that division?

You have likely watched many soccer games. When your team's ball crosses the center line, you cheer with joy, but when the ball comes back over the center line toward your side, how anxious do you feel? The spectators feel the same way. The larger the game, like the Olympics, the greater the anxiety proportional to the significance of the event and the relationships involved. When nations compete, the moment is very serious. That is why the athletes participating must give their all, for a single mistake can affect the whole. Have you experienced this? The ball can go in at once. Therefore, when the opponent kicks the ball and it is about to go in, the goalkeeper must move with all their strength toward the ball. But if they are foolishly looking elsewhere, how shocking would that be? However, in soccer, even if one goal is conceded, there is a chance to win again.

But the division of responsibilities placed before Adam and Eve, if violated even once, could become a terrifying pitfall for humanity for thousands of years. Knowing that Adam and Eve were in such a position, God warned them not to eat from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, anticipating the accusations from Satan. Yet they still ate from it; how do you think God's heart felt as He looked upon that?

Originally, they were born to be like that. Would He have supported them, saying, "Well done, well done"? In that moment of stumbling, God must have wanted to believe that they would not act that way.

How much did God's worried heart sway at that fork in the road? How much did He want to assert humanity's authority before the Fall? How earnest was His desire to establish that authority and subdue Satan? In such a painful position, humanity fell. This is not something that can be compensated for over a thousand years. Knowing that countless billions of beings would fall into the trap of death for eternity, how angry must God have felt? Humanity inflicted such a miserable wound. When we think of this, humanity is left speechless.

In the world, if a seventh-generation descendant born after the age of sixty dies, it would be despair upon despair. While youth may allow for more births, if that seventh-generation descendant, born with great hopes, does not grow well and dies, how anxious would the ancestors feel who wished to pass on the legacy?

Ancestors want to receive blessings that are not found in the world through their descendants, their bloodline. If their child dies, the parents would want to die alongside them. But Adam is not a seventh-generation descendant; he is the eternal descendant. God intended to establish a family centered on the one and only Adam to accomplish the great work of heaven and earth, but with Adam's death, how must God's heart have felt? What must He have thought when things went awry? Could it be compared to the anguish of wanting to marry but being unable to? Parents want to live together for a thousand years, but if their seventh-generation descendant is gravely ill and their life hangs by a thread, how would the parents feel? Imagine if your son or daughter were on the verge of death. Would the parents not scream? If the parents had a way to save their dying child, they would abandon all pride and dignity to use that method. Even if it meant becoming a servant to some enemy, if it could save their child, they would do it. Do you understand? If there is any way to save that child, parents do not think of pride or dignity.

If it means saving their child, parents would be willing to become servants. To find that one entity that can establish the purpose of the day, they would be willing to become a sacrifice that can resolve a thousand years of sorrow. If fallen parents feel this way, how much more would God?

When such sons and daughters cross over to eternal separation, the misery of God cannot be expressed in words. It is easy to say, as traditional churches do, not to eat from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil. But if it were that simple, the history of restoration would not have taken six thousand years. How much pain must God have felt as He watched His children enter into such a miserable and dark environment? Countless humans have come and gone on this earth, but no one has ever experienced such wounds. Jesus overcame the moment of death on the cross, but He did not reach the place where those wounds could be healed. We must recognize once again that God is such a being.

People go to church carrying Bibles, saying that if they believe in Jesus, they will go to heaven. They say, "Let's believe in Jesus and go to heaven," and it is astonishing. How wonderful it would be if it were that simple! If it were possible to go that way, why is Christianity increasingly failing? It is not that simple. To go to heaven, one must understand what God has gone through. If one goes to heaven without understanding this and later realizes that God was miserable, could they hold their head up? Those who go to heaven without knowing God's circumstances, could they lift their faces? Living without knowing the misery of God, can one say, "Father, let me go to heaven. Bless me"?

When such tremendous sorrow and deep anger are revealed in broad daylight, could one stand before such a God and say, "I am God's child"? If one could do that, they would truly be a Satan. Satan has betrayed God while trampling on such circumstances. If one can lift their face knowing God's situation, they are akin to the offspring of Satan. Such a person must go to hell. God is so miserable and wronged, yet in today's traditional churches, people say that the omniscient and omnipotent God has no reason to be sad. But the truth is, God is this miserable.

To enter heaven, one must understand this story on earth, and if they cannot resolve it with their own strength, they should at least become someone who sheds tears. If one laments their inability to resolve it, and becomes the protagonist of lamentation from a more pitiful position, would not God know that lamentation? When one laments in this way, it becomes a condition for establishing a connection with God. Being shameless will not establish that connection.

What happened when Adam and Eve fell? Did heaven and earth turn black or white? It is the same in the world, right? When a young couple separates or one dies, how much do they struggle? They may think they will not be like that, but everyone here is a candidate for that. No matter how capable a person is, even the most powerful person in South Korea is the same. There are no exceptions on that critical path. Raise your hand if you think you can make a deal there. No one, right? No matter how capable, how fat, how thin, or how close to death one may be, when they see that, they will shed tears, feel suffocated, have their hearts burst, and be shocked.

Then how must God's heart have felt? Would He have said, "Stop it. I will create again"? How wonderful that would be!

You will never forget when your son or daughter was born and then died. When that child said they wanted to eat something, why couldn't you provide it? When they wanted to wear something, why couldn't you buy it for them? All those stories of not being able to provide what they wanted become a source of sorrow. God has that heart, which is why He wishes to restore fallen humanity. If He did not have such a heart, there would be no restoration.

Do not boast of your dignity and authority. When Adam and Eve were in a position to do everything they wanted and desired, they could not fulfill it, and that is God's sorrow. It is because of that heart that He is carrying out the work of restoration. However, humanity was supposed to establish filial duty before God and set the laws of heaven and earth, but they failed to do so. Because of this, today's humanity, born in such a position, cannot help but groan in lamentation, curses, and dissatisfaction.

In order for us, who are in such a position, to stand on the side of heaven centered on God's public foundation, what must we do? We must not boast of our dignity and authority today. We must evoke the original heart of love that permeates our very bones, the heart of our nature before the Fall. We must not stand in the position of our fallen ancestors before God. Therefore, fallen parents must weep and shed tears. We, born as their descendants, must also suffer. We must become miserable. We must fall down. We must stand in a position of injustice. That is only natural. Centered on the love that is deeply hidden in our bones, longing for the Father who rejoiced before the Fall, embracing the wounds that Adam and Eve inflicted on God's heart through the Fall, and becoming a being who can offer the heart of unfallen nature, we cannot establish a connection with God.

That is why today's religions say to devote oneself until death. The Bible says, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, with all your mind, and with all your strength." (Mark 12:30)

Then what kind of position is that? It is not simply as a human born under the curse of God, but a position that knows how miserable the heart of the Father was, who wanted to love humanity by evoking the heart of nature that lies within our bones. That position, where one can empathize with such a heart, is the position of devotion. Only when one struggles to feel that can a connection with God be established. You must understand this clearly. This is the motivation to enter heaven.

When it is said to love with all your heart, if you say, "I am busy today, I have to go somewhere," is that all? And when you wanted to get married but said, "I should give up," or when you wanted to marry but said, "I should not marry," and turned away, is that all? What does it mean to love with all your heart, soul, and mind? What is the limit? You must understand this. Just living in a casual manner does not mean you are fulfilling this. You must clearly understand that limit. It surpasses the standard of heart that Adam and Eve had when they fell. They could not love God or care about His will. They also did not know what God's inner heart was like. Therefore, you must not stand irresponsibly after receiving the command.

Centered on the words of God in the Bible, you must invest your whole being with a seriousness greater than Adam's. Your heart must be earnest, like a bomb flying toward its target, ready to explode. God hopes that not only the standard of devotion that crosses the line of death will be met, but that all people will sing of love centered on God and be embraced in God's bosom, surpassing that standard.

God is a wronged and indignant being. Who is to blame for that? It is because of me. You may think it is not you. You may wonder what relationship you have with your ancestors from thousands of years ago, but that is not true. You have likely seen a withered tree that has only a single sprout left. Whether it is a ginkgo or a zelkova, when asked how old that sprout is, would you say it is three months old because it sprouted this spring? Would you not say that its age began from the roots planted by your grandfather?

Who is like that sprout of the withered tree? It is you. Then how old are you? Do not think of yourself as fifteen or twenty. You must add six thousand years to the age you think you are. Since six thousand years is a burden, you simply think of yourself as fifteen or twenty. Six thousand years are all the same. In truth, if you ask how old you are, you should say, "I am six thousand and something years old." You may wonder where such a person exists, but in the world of the heart, that is how it is.

For believers, an extremely miserable position is also necessary. You may have lived, but you are like a pine tree that has only one root left, hanging upside down on a cliff or a hillside after being battered by a storm. Whether it is a pine or a willow or a mulberry tree... When the storm continues to rage, how must those trees feel? Would they wish for the rain to stop? Think about it. Would they wish for it to stop? Have you ever wished so earnestly for life? Where can there be anything more miserable than that? If only the roots were alive, there might be hope, but this tree has completely rotted away, like a soft radish... Even if leaves are attached to that radish top, it will ultimately rot. Even if the owner pulls it out, it will all go into the barn.

You are in such a state. The same goes for those who believe in Christianity today. The roots are hanging precariously on the hillside, and the body is falling into the sea, yet they say they want to live there. Is that not pitiful? Can one dance and rejoice in such a state? No matter how much life force one boasts, when they see that wall above them...
If we do not take root somewhere, we have no way to survive. Therefore, we must seek out our roots. This means we must cut down the entire tree and take the new branches that sprout from the roots. For a sprout to emerge here, we must cut off the old self. Only with such a mindset can we leave behind the seeds. If we simply cut ourselves off, it will lead to disaster. If we insist that we must live, everything will end up in ruin without a trace.

When looking at a large ship encountering a storm at sea, when the waves are so high that the mast is not visible, one might think the ship has sunk, and when it reappears, a sigh of relief escapes, right? How does that feel? Does it resonate with you? If it feels that way for those watching, how must it be for those on board? Have you thought about how the captain feels? You might think, "You are lucky to be in that situation." When the ship is going down, the captain's heart must be pounding, and he must be calling out to God, "Oh God, I am going to die." Each time the ship goes under the waves, he must cry out to God, and each time it rises, he must express gratitude. Wouldn't that be the case? Think about it.

People need such experiences. They must find themselves in extreme and miserable situations. Think about Jesus, carrying the cross and heading to Golgotha while being mocked. The Jews mocked Jesus, saying, "What a disgrace! The son of a carpenter!" If you had been there, what would you have said to Jesus? You would have likely joined in the insults. Today, if someone were to say to Jesus, "You disgrace!" it would cause an uproar, but back then, people had no choice but to react that way. Do you think the Jews crucified Jesus because they were all inferior to you?

What about the Messiah, who had been awaited for thousands of years? He gathered people and wandered from town to town, being chased away. The Jews did not see this Jesus as the Messiah. However, because Jesus was in the position of a son who had to carry God's deep feelings, he considered persecution to be a natural consequence.

When we see Jesus being crowded, beaten, mistreated, and mocked, God could not help but feel compassion for him. Of course, in the Garden of Gethsemane, he prayed, "If it is possible, let this cup pass from me," but that was a prayer for humanity. However, once the decision was made, he accepted it all. A general with the appearance of a brave man would prefer to die not by a rifle but by an atomic bomb. Similarly, Jesus did not think that the national curses and mockery were too great. He believed that the path of heavenly principles he had to walk could not be confused or obstructed by anything you do.

You must clearly understand that God is a sorrowful being. Jesus, having descended from the original Adam and Eve, had the inner feelings that could surpass God's sorrow. He boldly stepped into the place of death, where his honor and glory could be lost in an instant, embracing God, and resolved to live with God whether he died or lived. Because of this resolution, God was able to comfort Jesus instead. This is how the foundation of heaven was established on this earth. Without a foundation that can receive comfort from God, the unification of the world cannot be achieved. When you think about this, you must understand that God is a sorrowful being.

Even when you go to the theater to watch a movie, you must stand in a serious position and feel that it is not someone else's issue but your own. If you feel that it is an enemy that hinders your path of faith, then when some wicked group appears, you should have the mindset to drive them away, and it would not be a sin to go to the theater. If you go with such a mindset, it is okay to go to places even worse than the theater.

If you go to a den of villains, even if you have to disguise yourself as a con artist, if you have the confidence that you can pull them up, and if you set out with the determination to strike down all enemies in one blow, you will be raised as a hero of God. Such a person becomes a sacrificial offering wherever they go. Do you think that will happen? "I think so." Then how much do you think it will happen? Think about it. Can you really kill and cut them down? You might think it would be easy, but that place is serious. The person speaking here is serious too. You may not realize it, but I am risking my life. Without sowing life, you cannot reap the seeds of life. It is said that you reap what you sow. Because God came to find humanity with such feelings, those with such feelings have helped develop history until now. Those people are on God's side.

God is a being who has lost everything and is sorrowful. If a person dies from a naturally occurring illness, it might be acceptable, but they were warned that eating would lead to death, yet they foolishly ate. How resentful must that be to see? They were told that eating would lead to death. They were told they would surely die. Even after being warned, they still chose to eat it. Humans tend to do more of what they are told not to do.

If you say, "Don't come to the Unification Church," they will come even more. If you say, "Come, come," they might not come, but if you hit them with a stick and tell them not to come, they will be sitting there at dawn. You might wonder what time the teacher will come out with a stick. Because of this frog-like nature, things have gone awry. So, would God look at it and say, "Well done. That could happen"? 

If that were the case, how nice would it be? If you go mindlessly to the edge of a cliff, you can only die. You become a corpse.

What law can be established by believing in Jesus? The law of love can be established. If there is a bride and groom who, despite all opposition from the neighborhood and even from parents and siblings, are determined to overcome all opposition and have a wedding ceremony, and if the bride says to the groom, "I will go to another man for a while, so please wait," what would happen? Would that statement be accepted? Absolutely not. God has faced such situations. If you do such things and love God, will God meet you again? You become an enemy. You become a disgrace. Is there anyone worse than that in the world? There is no one worse than that, even if you look around the world.

Would God say to such a person, "You did that because you didn't know the law of love, so now you should stop"? Would that be acceptable? It cannot be accepted. That is why problems arise. Killing one person can be forgiven hundreds or thousands of times. The only relative center that can stand before God's love has shattered the law of love, so where can it be found? To establish this, Jesus brought the religion of love. The reason Christianity today cries out for love is precisely that. Yet, despite that, you say that you ate the forbidden fruit and died? You are darker than a blind person wandering at night. How easy would it be to believe like that? If so, how comfortable would the teacher of the Unification Church be?

So how can we restore God's dignity? We must find sons and daughters who can be loved more than when the fall occurred. To do this, we must have a faith that is higher than that of Adam and Eve at that time. In terms of heart and character, we must be above Adam and Eve. When Satan said, "Did God say to eat the forbidden fruit?" and tempted them by saying that their eyes would be opened, we must not become those who fall into that trap. At this time, we must be better than Adam and Eve, and in character, we must be able to say to Satan, "Who are you, you disgrace! You are a servant." We must also be able to ask, "Who is the master of love?" in our hearts.

So what does the Unification Church want to do today? It wants to create people who are above that level of faith. Is that good or bad? Is it good? How good is it? If you can become such a person, no matter how you express your gratitude, it will never be enough. If that is a lie, then you can die being hit by a pile of stones, but if it is the truth, how much gratitude should you express? You should be grateful until you die and are resurrected. If that happens, how joyful would God be?

You must become someone who has no shame in greeting the morning of resurrection that Jesus rejoiced in. When Mary Magdalene met the resurrected Jesus, she could not approach him before the time came and said, "Do not touch me." Only those who can taste the morning of resurrection can stand before the Father. To do so, you must understand that you need to feel the pain of death.

In believing in God, you must believe absolutely. Humanity, burdened by the history of disbelief, must believe whether it is life or death. Only by believing in this way can you go to heaven. Just going to church with the Bible does not mean you believe in Jesus. Even if you carry the cross and go over Golgotha, you must believe that you will resurrect! You must believe more actively than anyone else.

In the past, Satan crossed the boundary and spoke to Adam and Eve. But today, a believer must have authority and character, making Satan afraid to approach them. They must be the kind of person who can make the archangel afraid to come before them. Would those who pray a lot be under Satan's dominion? They must be the kind of person with sincere content that Satan cannot appear before them.

Where does the heart start? Among you here, there may be some young men and women. Who do you think is the protagonist of the heart? You might think that when you get married, your husband is the protagonist, and your wife is the protagonist, but that is not true. The root of the heart, the protagonist of the heart, is God.

Thus, humanity must live in the womb. The role of religion is to help us connect to that womb life. That is why true religion teaches us about womb life. Does the Unification Church also engage in womb life? Do you want it or not?

So how do we achieve that? We must become people who can surpass the standard of Adam and Eve in character. The same goes for the heart. If we stand in a position that brings about injustice to God, causing Him to be sorrowful, how sorrowful must God be? It is already unforgivable to have inflicted wounds until now, so how can we continue to bring misery again? We must have the heart that says, "Even if I die, I cannot walk that path." Only with such a standard of heart can we align with God and stand on God's side.

So what kind of being is God? Do you think He is a God who sits on a throne receiving glory? That is not the case. What has God done for fallen humanity until now? He has been weeping every day to save this humanity. This is the image of God leading humanity from such a standpoint. God is a being who is this miserable. To save humanity that has fallen into misery, God is waking up the sleeping humanity, calling out, "Come! Come!" However, it does not work that way. There must be a division of responsibility, and how hard it must have been for God to work from a position where He cannot delegate that responsibility!

God has been guiding the outcasts of the world. When we look at those who knock on the door of religion today, seeking the true path, we see many outcasts in the world. Even if Unification Church members seem to sit quietly, they are all bruised people from the world. They are those who have fallen and stumbled in this era and this world. They are people who feel uncomfortable at home, uncomfortable at school, and dissatisfied with what they see in play, with society, and with the world. They cannot sweep it all away, so they are struggling. Seeing this, it seems more appealing to say, "I will go cleanly away," during the youth period. They feel it is better to just leave. It is frustrating to have to bow down to those who are utterly foolish, isn't it? Especially simple young women tend to do such things. They think that is smart. But that is not what I am saying to do. If you do that, you will go to hell. Even those standing here have felt that way many times.

Such experiences must be endured. However, that is not the problem. The question is whether, after doing so, you will encounter rocky paths or a peaceful wilderness in your life journey.

When you look into the hearts of those who have entered the Unification Church, you will find that they are all bruised, with holes and a stamp of defeat on their life paths. It is not just one or two; there are holes all over the place. When you see this, how miserable must God feel? Until now, when God has been guiding humanity to save them, what kind of people has He centered His providence around? He has centered His providence around trash-like humans. How shocking is that? Those who think they are great have all run away, leaving behind those who are utterly foolish, wounded, disabled, and deformed. God has been guiding His providence around those who are not all-rounders but all-round failures.

Not knowing this, you may have entered the Unification Church thinking, "Why don't they recognize me for working for the purpose?" But you should reflect on whether you are truly that self. You should feel your heart racing, worried that you might be driven away, but instead, there are those who want to drive others away, and that is the problem.

A place that gathers trash and regenerates it is called a regeneration center. The church signifies a place where humans can be repaired again. So what kind of church is the Unification Church? It is a church that regenerates everything. It is a place that regenerates everything.

What must be centered upon for restoration? Love alone is not enough. Since the fall occurred because of love, to restore it, the love must be greater than the love before the fall. That is the love after restoration.

So can I bring forth that love? Can humans bring it forth by themselves? They cannot. Then who will do it? It is the parents. God will bring it forth. Therefore, you must be grafted onto this. You must be grafted onto God, who is different in both root and stem. You must understand how much God has walked a miserable path to enable this grafting.

When you think about that, do you think God lived with a smile, or did He live with a pounding heart and weeping? When you lose a child you have raised and hold that child in your arms, shedding tears, how much pain must the Father have felt when He experienced such things? You must be grateful for understanding how great that pain was. You must recognize that He allowed such things to happen for your salvation. You must feel that everything the Father has done through the historical process is not someone else's business but your own. You must think of all the events that have occurred over 6,000 years as your own, not someone else's.
What it means is that your salvation signifies the victory of the entire 6,000-year historical course. When you achieve victory, it means that all the historical accumulations of 6,000 years can enter an era of resurrection. If that were to happen, how delighted would God be?

God's intention to deny everything and call me to Him
When Adam and Eve fell, God was miserable, but when He worked providentially to find Adam and Eve again, He was even more miserable. God, who was expelled and betrayed by His children, looking at the situation where He was embraced by the enemy and living in a state of desperation, what must have been His condition? 

What would Satan have said upon seeing this? 
"Why has God become like that? Your son has become like this. Look, he is with me." He would have laughed. The very environment in which humans live becomes the material for Satan to mock God. If we live well with God, true internal governance would dwell there, but because we have become one with Satan, we have become materials that can be treated like Satan before God. That is why God said that He cannot come to me without completely severing all ties and settling everything. He cannot return to me without loving me more than anyone else.

From this perspective, have we struggled to fulfill our duty of filial piety and loyalty before God today? Until now, we have just lived habitually. Our internal feelings, soaked in the stage of life, have become materials for Satan to accuse us before God. Therefore, although God came to find humanity with joy, He ended up bearing the cross again, embracing sorrow and shedding tears.

When I think that the God who was saddened by the fall of the human ancestors 6,000 years ago is shedding tears again because of my meeting with Him, we must understand how miserable God is. That is why God comes bearing the cross of the heart, the cross of the heart.

Standing on the side of heaven
In the family of Adam, how much effort did God exert to restore Adam's family through Abel, centering on Cain and Abel, leaving behind the fallen Adam and Eve? How long did He long for these children to have the connection to faithfully serve Him with sincere hearts? Did He wait just a day or two? He waited for decades.

In that process, how anxious must the Father's heart have been when He designated a certain day to restore? But when this was shattered by Cain, how must have the Father's heart felt? After 1,600 years, when it came to Noah, how much pain did the Father's heart endure while making Noah suffer for 120 years to restore that situation? How much did He long for those 120 years to pass? Noah must have found those 120 years tedious, but how much more tedious was it for God, who knew and waited for that time? Noah could believe in God and had God as a comforting object when he followed His commands. However, God had no one to comfort Him. He was looking at Noah, who could abandon God at any moment and leave marks of betrayal on God's heart. For Noah, it was 120 years, but for God watching this, a day must have felt like a thousand years.

After all the hard work culminated in a foundation to establish God's will, when everything collapsed due to Ham's mistake, Satan must have been delighted, but God had to turn away, forgetting all circumstances, so how heart-wrenching must that have been? Even if that was okay, how much effort did God exert to bring Abraham, the son of His beloved Sarah, out of the Gentiles 400 years later to rectify Ham's mistake? And if Abraham had not complied when told to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, God would have had to leave that place as well. You must clearly understand that there was such a heartbreaking story. When God found Abraham and took a step forward, knowing that if Abraham did not move according to God's command, all of history's efforts would be in vain, how must have God's heart felt at that moment?

Reflecting on the historical resentment of the ancestors from Adam's time to that point, how much did God long for Abraham not to betray Him as He sought a day to step over that resentment? It would be fortunate if Abraham understood God's heart and welcomed Him, but how anxious must God have been, thinking, "What if he does not?"

God promised, "Your descendants will be as numerous as the stars in the sky and the sand on the seashore," but when He prepared offerings to approach Him with great aspirations and hopes, how anxious must the Father's heart have been? 

Think about God's anxiety and sorrow in the restoration process.
Abraham was in a position where he had to put forth all his sincerity and think a thousand or ten thousand times. Yet, even while splitting the oxen and sheep, he did not split the doves, allowing Satan to invade, and witnessing everything he had longed for over 2,000 years come to an end in an instant, how resentful must God's heart have been? To restore these things, how must have God's heart felt when He commanded Abraham to offer his beloved son Isaac as a sacrifice? Even if Abraham had the heart to obey ten times, what if Isaac had opposed him, saying, "What kind of command is this? This old man must be crazy"? How anxious must God's heart have been, knowing that neither parent nor child could oppose this?

When God told Abraham to offer Isaac as a sacrifice, how much sorrow must He have felt while giving that command? He must have thought a thousand or ten thousand times. God knows that if the command is not accepted, resentment will linger in the history of 2,000 years. Therefore, when He called out, "Abraham!" there was a deep story behind that voice. When Abraham went to offer the sacrifice, Satan was at a crossroads, wondering whether his descendants would be defeated in the historical course of a thousand years or whether history would be extended. Thus, Satan made every effort to disrupt this.

You must understand how poignant God's voice was when He placed Abraham in such a decisive battleground. Also, how sorrowful must God have felt watching Abraham walk for three days toward Mount Moriah with his child? God knew that whether things went well or poorly in that environment would determine the fate of thousands or even tens of thousands of years of history. If the ignorant Isaac had opposed his father at that moment, God would not have been able to accept him as a sacrifice. If I were to offer you as a sacrifice, would you remain silent?

Isaac, even in the place where he was about to be stabbed with a knife, obeyed his father like a lamb, without any complaints, thus cutting off the path for Satan to accuse. Adam fell into the way of death by betraying God's word for personal glory, happiness, and desires. However, regarding Isaac and Abraham's sincerity, who were offered as sacrifices without a word of complaint, Satan could not accuse them. Here, the history of Abraham, the ancestor of faith, began. 

How sorrowful must God have been until that decisive moment? A new morning of victory that could be boasted before humanity for thousands of years was about to arrive, and the heart of sorrow was passing, revealing a hopeful beginning where joy could sprout. In other words, sorrow passed away, and because a day of joy stronger than that sorrow was coming, the history of the founding of Israel began from that time.

The world of darkness that began due to Adam's fall was set to start a world that could be welcomed with joy due to Abraham's obedience to God's command. Only then could Abraham, bearing the name of the ancestor of faith, begin a new historical journey on this earth.

However, because there were remnants of Satan's accusations, Jacob and Esau had to fight again. What if Jacob had fought with Laban for 21 years, grabbing him by the collar? That could not happen. He was scorned, despised, and lost everything, but he longed for the day when his father's blessing would be fulfilled, and his hope for that blessing was greater than anything in the world, allowing him to overcome all difficulties.

Jacob's perseverance
What did Jacob deeply feel during this time? That there was no one in the world to trust. He could not trust his uncle, relatives, or anyone. So, the more he entered into that opposing environment, the more he thought about embracing God entirely as his own. For 21 years, he made God his possession, the owner of his heart, the substitute for his parents, and the king of his homeland on the foundation of his heart.

For Jacob, who understood this internal situation deeply, external wealth was not an issue. Even if he suffered external loss, he knew that God's internal wealth was being accumulated within him, so he endured being driven away and rejected for 21 years. However, his love for his homeland and respect for being a blessed descendant of Abraham did not change. Because even Satan recognized that he loved his value as a descendant of blessed Abraham more than anyone else, Jacob could not be deprived of the banner of blessing, and no one could accuse him.

When Jacob returned home, how heart-wrenching must God have felt when He had to send an angel to Jacob to make a final decision? This was because the first fall occurred through the archangel Lucifer, and to resolve this, the spiritual aspect had to be addressed first before victory could be achieved in the physical battle, so God sent an angel to wrestle with Jacob.

In this situation, Jacob fought with all his might, even as his bones were dislocated. He thought, "The efforts I have made for 21 years are being judged in this fight! Whether I win or lose in this one night of struggle determines my life's fate and the foundation of Israel's blessing!" He fought for his life, knowing that the angel had come as God's messenger. 

When the angel came, Jacob recognized that he had come as God's messenger. Therefore, when he asked whether the angel had come to destroy him or to bless him, and the angel replied that he had come to bless him, Jacob asked, "If you are here to bless me, why can't you just give it to me?" The angel replied that there were responsibilities to share, so it could not be given freely. In other words, if Jacob did not wrestle and win, the blessing could not be given. In other words, if he did not fight for his life, it could not be given. When that condition was set, Jacob resolved, "Even if my fingers break and my arms break, I will never give in."

How long did this last? All night long. He fought with the determination that he would not let go until he died. God was present, and Satan was present. But how anxious must Jacob have felt in that decisive moment? Even when the angel struck his hip and dislocated it, Jacob did not let go. He was determined that whether he died or the angel died, neither would he let go. How many hours do you think this lasted? Ten minutes? One hour? Two hours? More than seven hours. Yet Jacob was absolutely unwilling to yield. In the midst of this, how heart-wrenching must God's heart have been? God wanted to tell Jacob not to yield because the angel was fighting on behalf of Satan, but He could not, so think about how anxious He must have been during that time.

As time passed and the final decision was made, when the angel could not shake Jacob off, both God and Satan recognized him. Only when Jacob stood in that position could the angel acknowledge him, and he finally received the name Israel.

When Jacob triumphed over the angel and received the name Israel, what happened in the heavenly world? They released their held breaths and cheered. The deep sigh of sorrow that had accumulated in their hearts was not just a matter of the 2,000 years of history. Jacob's heart connection, which allowed him to embrace God for 20 years while shedding tears, was able to surpass the connection that Adam and Eve had when they fell, allowing him to receive the title of Israel.

How much resentment must God have felt until that time? Even if He shed tears repeatedly, He could not comfort the heart burdened by sin that we humans bear. Because we bear this historical debt, even offering a million sacrifices cannot repay it. How many times do we betray God in the present?

If you feel that the one who bears the burden of sorrow is your Father, then when you look at this, how great must be the burden of God, who must save all this reality and restore the world? When you think of this, even if you are a frail woman or a weak person, you must struggle to take on even a part of that burden. Unless there is a movement on this earth to take responsibility for that place, even if it means dragging your wounded body, we cannot prepare a foundation for the earthly paradise that can comfort God, who comes bearing the historical resentment.

Who is the one who has come bearing the burden of sorrow and the cross of the heart? He is not some old grandfather or a stepfather. He is a Father who must enjoy glory for thousands and tens of thousands of years, receive love, and live eternally in happiness with His children. The Unification Church members must recognize that such a Father is in such a miserable position. 

You must understand that the Unification group, which has gathered with the mission to approach God, who comes bearing the historical resentment, must embrace Him and say, "Father, I now understand; Father, I have come; Father, I will now follow you; Father, please command me," and strive to embody that.

From the time Jacob established the foundation of victory as Israel through Abraham and Isaac until Jesus came, how much humiliation did the Israelite people endure? How much were they chased and oppressed? God could not abandon such a people. From the perspective of historical connections, He could not forget the times when they comforted Him even in sorrow, so whenever the Israelite people went astray, He repeatedly intervened, offering blessings and prayers thousands and thousands of times. However, due to the sin of killing Jesus, they became a people who have wandered for 2,000 years.
Two thousand years later, until the Israelite people are equipped with a new Israelite authority, God did not leave them as a lost nation. For two thousand years, God's heart, watching over the wandering Israelite people, was intertwined with the grief of four thousand years of history. However, despite their cries and wandering, enduring oppression and massacre before countless nations and humanity, they have served God.

Because that nation existed, the providence of restoration could be pioneered, and also, because it is pitiful that God has not yet sent the Messiah He promised, while still believing in the old promises and waiting, God has gathered that nation again and protected them from their enemies in the Arab world. How much effort must God have put in to do this? You must understand that He has been anxious to protect a flock of sheep among a pack of wolves.

The fact that Israel fought against the Arab world and achieved victory in six days was due to God's power and protection. Without God's power and protection, it would have been absolutely impossible. This is recognized by all as a miracle of the 20th century. So how could this miracle occur? It happened because God was working behind the scenes. Because the heart of the Israelite people seeking God and the heart of God wanting to relate to such Israelites were intertwined, a victorious foundation was laid to defeat the enemies surrounding them. That is why Israel was able to raise the flag of liberation to the world.

The Israelite people, who brought sorrow before God two thousand years ago, have now established a nation and raised a new flag to praise God, which serves as good evidence that God has protected them. It also serves as good evidence that God does not abandon nations and future generations.

The Correct Attitude for Unification Church Members
Today, you have entered the Unification Church. So what is the Unification Church? It is not to comfort God, who has come out with sorrow for two thousand years from Adam to Abraham. For four thousand years, God sent the Messiah to the Israelite people, who were wandering before various nations, to prepare a global foundation for the restoration, but the Israelite people lost this. That is why the members of the Unification Church have been called together to take responsibility for the historical whole to restore this two thousand years of history.

When we bow down and pray before the Father today, we must call upon Him with a choked voice and a heart that aches. Father, who has been filled with countless grievances and sorrows because of me for six thousand years, who has endured countless wounds, injustices, and mockery before countless enemies, when we think of You, who is filled with countless grievances, wounds, and miserable stories, we must be able to melt Your heart even if we become a hot lump of fire. However, when we think of ourselves as children of lamentation and curses who cannot do that, what can we do to comfort that Father? We are those who must cry out all night in agony and lament without being able to relieve our grievances. Nevertheless, where have all those feelings gone?

You must understand that God has gone through countless histories to prepare an environment where the flag of unification can be planted. You must know that there have been countless days that could not be spoken to anyone. If there is someone who is being treated poorly at a door, they must understand that there is a God who has faced circumstances far worse than that. When our nation is in a miserable environment, we must recognize that the Israelite people have gone through an even more miserable national environment. Furthermore, we must understand that God has come to find people even from a position more painful and miserable than that, holding onto hope. We must recognize that such circumstances of God have been inherited to us today through bloodlines.

Because we are inheriting this historical foundation of grief, we cannot help but feel guilt after eating, and we cannot help but shed tears of repentance after sleeping. This is the philosophy of life and attitude of Unification Church members. We are in a position where we cannot be happy even when we eat, cannot be happy even when we see clothes, and cannot smile even when we look at our surroundings. We must understand how much God has suffered in misery, hunger, oppression, and mockery.

We must welcome such a God. We must serve such a Father. We must pray to become children who can dedicate ourselves to relieving the heart of the Father, who has been filled with grief for six thousand years. We must appeal to God to become those who can inherit the true love of the Father, which has been cherished for six thousand years.

We have not overcome difficult circumstances. We have not been able to endure. We have not even overcome the seven-year course. Yet we are a group with cursed lips that have been busy judging God. We must now become those who can curse ourselves for having become such shameless beings. We must seek ways to remove the traces of God's grief while struggling and lamenting. If there is a way to do this, we must struggle to the point of dying a thousand or ten thousand times; this is the path that Unification Church members must take. You must become a son or daughter who can do that, and you must become a family that can do that. Who will be the son who can do that, and who will be the daughter who can do that? Without becoming such beings, you cannot enter the Kingdom of God. A family made up of such sons and daughters, a tribe made up of such families, a nation made up of such tribes, and a world made up of such nations must exist to enter the Kingdom of God.

Today, you must bear the cross of the heart that God must bear. Even if your body is torn and becomes food for beggars and eagles, you must walk that path. However, God, despite being in a position where He cannot do that, has been struggling until now, forgetting His dignity and position, to save humanity.

True Filial Piety
You must become people who can call upon the Father from the position of heaven, who can represent the Father's position from the position of heaven, and who can confront enemies on behalf of the Father from the position of heaven. You must understand how much the Father is searching for such people. If there is such a son, He wants to hold him tightly until his bones crumble, and if there is such a daughter, He wants to spend the night sharing His story. Who will relieve the grief that is bound in the heart of such a Father? It is you. Thus, God should be able to proclaim to the whole world that He has seen a day of happiness because of your family, that He has relieved His grief because of your family, and that He has welcomed a day of hope because of you. You must understand that only when such a day arrives can the Kingdom of Heaven be opened on this earth.

So what should we think about today? We must not stand on our side against God. Today, God is looking for those who will say, "Even if I must sacrifice myself, please forgive the sins of the nation." He is looking for those who will say, "Even if I must sacrifice myself, please forgive the sins of the world." If there is someone who, while feeling the pain of being sacrificed, appeals for the forgiveness of the sins of the nation and the world, that person will become one who can inherit the whole world.

Until today, people have all worked centered around themselves. "Me, me, me..." How long will this self-centeredness last? Because they centered on themselves, all the places where they could stand have been shattered. There have been all sorts of events. The teacher often prays alone. You do not know the circumstances in which God has communicated His situation and held onto the teacher. That is a situation only I can know. How could God, who created this vast universe, have become a God who comes to a mere individual to plead for His own misery? You must understand that God is working hard to create His sons and daughters, even if it means disregarding His dignity and position.

God is longing for a son who can be centered on Him, a son who can be believed in for thousands and tens of thousands of years, a son who is worthy of praise for millions of years. He is a Father who is anxiously waiting for Adam to revive. But why has He become a sorrowful Father who cannot become a Father who can sing of eternal happiness centered around beloved sons and daughters? Someone who can serve such a Father must arise from anywhere on this earth. If you cannot do that, you must at least pray to become an environment where that can happen. You must be willing to be scorned, persecuted, and shackled.

Where is there anyone who can protect God's sons and daughters for God's sake? Where is there anyone who can protect that family for God, and where is there anyone who can stand on God's side to protect tribes and nations? Where is there a son or daughter who can run the world with the authority of a son on behalf of the Father? No one has appeared who can do that before the Father, whom He has been waiting for since ancient times. However, we must become such sons and daughters, and even if it means becoming a sacrifice a thousand or ten thousand times in our lifetime, we must become the foundation and cornerstone for that. However, despite this, we are making excuses while God is grieving, and that is a cursed situation.

Let us carry the emotional cross on behalf of God.
Today, the teacher prayed and wept before the Father. I realized that He is a Father with a history of grief in the flowing years, but I have not been able to comfort such a Father, nor have I been able to establish authority before the nation, nor have I been able to subdue the nation and the world to offer them to the Father, creating a pitiful situation. I wanted to quickly fulfill the Father's will and proudly present you as beloved sons and daughters before all people, but because that has been delayed, many have grown weary and fallen away.

When the teacher travels to the provinces, I think of those I used to meet and talk to while evangelizing in alleys or on the roadside. However, while the foundation remains, those people have disappeared, making me think of the story of the Father who has walked the path of restoration for thousands of years. Will you become someone who begs the Father to repay a debt, or someone who asks for wages while avoiding the Father's eyes and stealing His possessions? You must recognize your own shame for not having fulfilled your responsibilities until now and strive to become a stepping stone for the fulfillment of God's ideals and will, struggling for the final victory.

You must pray to become a person of heaven when you open your eyes. You must struggle to stand on the side of heaven, to be scorned on the side of heaven, to suffer injustice on the side of heaven, and to leave a connection with your tribe on the side of heaven.

Until now, the path the Unification Church has walked has been miserable. It has come out with unspeakable stories and uncontrollable circumstances. Therefore, you can understand what the situation of heaven is like, what the anger of heaven is like, and what the internal affairs of heaven are like. A person is not born to live a hundred or a thousand years on this earth; life is like a fleeting dew, and we must not leave behind a tower of God's curses.

When you die, you must leave behind comrades or sons and daughters who can come to your grave with flowers and cry out, "Father! Your beloved son is leaving. Who will love this land that your son loved, who will save this nation, and who will save this altar?" If you do not do that, you cannot go before God. Regardless of the circumstances, you must not forget that humanity must comfort the Father with tears. All must unite and stand on the side of heaven, struggling to prepare a foundation where God can rest on this earth for thousands and tens of thousands of years, and even if that means dying in the process, that will not be a grievance.

You must recognize that Jesus also struggled to establish his integrity as he walked toward the path of the cross. What does it mean to have a spear wound in Jesus' side, and what does it mean to have a crown of thorns on His head? However, Jesus knew that the wounds inflicted on God's heart were greater than the painful wounds on His own body, so He shed blood to comfort the Father's heart and sought to relieve the Father's grief with His wounded heart. You must understand that it was this heart that allowed Him to resurrect.

Therefore, today, we Unification Church members must bear the emotional cross on behalf of God. I hope that all of you will be responsible for the side of heaven, live on the side of heaven, and be able to resurrect on the side of heaven, and I ask you to remember this moment.

<Prayer> In the long history, when has there been a day for the Father, when has there been a day for parents, when has there been a day for children, and when has there been a day for all things? When I think that these days were determined through the group of unification that was pitifully persecuted and chased, I sincerely thank the Father who has worked in history.

Father, now the first seven-year course has ended, and the time to embark on the second seven-year course is approaching us. A chaotic world is about to come before us. We see that those who opposed us in the world are being broken down.

Father, please allow the day of liberation and the day of freedom to come quickly for your sons and daughters who are struggling to embrace your heart, having cast aside all dignity and face. Father! The children of yours who are here today know how dire the situation of heaven is, so please allow us to become transformed sons and transformed daughters.

I thank you for being with us today. Please embrace your children scattered throughout South Korea in your bosom. I earnestly hope that you will look upon us with compassion and not abandon us. Please remember your children scattered throughout the world, and bless them so that they may only see a day of victory wherever they go.

Father, I know that your children who remain must not leave. In the midst of a chaotic world, please make them your children who can dedicate themselves to you and devote their hearts to you. Please allow us to repent of our past shortcomings and fulfill our duty of loyalty before you, and may the sincerity we offer allow all people to receive blessings, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

I believe that the day of victory will come before us, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents.
I humbly offer this in reverence to the Holy Name. Amen.  
14)  
New Motivation  
<Summary of the Message> Humanity cannot establish a new motivation without standing in the position prior to the Fall. Furthermore, one cannot establish a new motivation without having the power to surpass the attacks of Satan and standing on God's side. This is because this time is a confrontation between the world of evil centered on Satan and the world of good centered on God.  
What will be the foundation for future national, state, and global traditions? This is the mission that you, who have started from the position of God's children, must undertake. The difficult tasks have been entrusted to God, while the easier ones have been taken on by ourselves, and this has been the path we have walked until today.  
The second seven-year course is a period for which each of you must take responsibility. Therefore, this course is different from the previous seven-year course, which was carried out under the responsibility of parents. That is why those who did not obey the commands have been removed.  
The teacher had to undergo trials of the three eras (Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent), three nations (Japan, communist nations, and democratic nations), three governments (Korea), and three denominations, and had to go through the three generations (36, 72, 120 families).  
The teacher has walked alone through the night until now and has now welcomed the morning. This is the responsibility of all of you to practice these words.  
July 7, 1968 (Sunday) morning, former headquarters church.  
* This message has been organized from notes taken by former Association President Yoo Woo-won.  
15)  
Our Pride  
Romans 8:36-39  
<Prayer (I)> Father! Please allow us to discover ourselves by understanding Your heart in the stillness. The more we think, the more we cannot help but realize how distant we are from Your will. Because the ancestors of humanity forsook You and fell into the path of destruction, we were born as descendants who must perish forever, and when we realize that we have left a gap that is so hard to narrow in our search for You, we discover once again that there is nothing we can do.  
When we think of ourselves, born from the roots of death and entangled in the world of death in the past and present, we cannot help but find ourselves too far from belonging to You, Father. Therefore, we know that we need Your loving hand and the touch of Your power.  
Father, we deeply possess the bond of nature. This is what we have inherited from You, and we know that this bond means we cannot do without You.  
To establish this bond, You have awakened us through the historical process, and even now, Your work for this continues at this time, so please do not let us forget this fact.  
July 7, 1968 (Sunday), former headquarters church.  
240 Our Pride  
Please allow us to know the earnest desires that our nature is crying out for, and let us understand that our nature truly wants to establish a relationship with You, Father. Also, let us realize that the bitter roots of the enemy, which oppose our nature, surround us.  
Let us understand that our nature must manifest Your power, and we earnestly wish for the beginning of life that can step over all the entangled bonds of death, held by Your powerful hand, Father.  
As we have come through a long history, we have come to know how much effort You have put in, and we also understand how great Your sorrow has been in embracing humanity until now. We have also come to know that You are trying to resolve the grievances accumulated in the historical process through humanity. However, while the resolution for the whole is important, we must first resurrect ourselves before our families, tribes, and nations can be resurrected, so please allow us to clearly understand that You desire a resolution for our individual selves.  
Today, we have gathered here not as a family of the whole but as individuals before Your presence, Father. Now, please allow each of us to hear once again the commands You give, and let us be able to firmly instill in our hearts the single-mindedness You desire.  
Father, please raise a new history through each of us that can remove all elements of sin. We wish to be offered to You as true sons and daughters, whom You wanted to embrace in a place where we can align with Your heart, align in our lives, and align with the eternal future from a position of desire. However, we find ourselves too lacking and insufficient for that, and we must become Your sons and daughters who can feel a sense of shame.  
Please do not let us become sons and daughters who forget our shame and do not know how to be ashamed before You, Father. When our individual selves are viewed in light of the will of unification, we must clearly state that we are unworthy of forgiveness from You, God, and reveal the reasons for that, so that at this time, we can feel the heart of Your compassionate heart with a shameful heart and have a sincere desire to do so.  
We have come knocking on the door of unification according to Your will, Father. Until now, we have heard and learned the words that are taught here. However, we must realize that without becoming the substance that can communicate through the words, we have no relationship with You, God, and we should not exist as words and as ourselves separately.  
Please allow us to understand that in order to establish ourselves as the substance of the words, we must stand in a position where we can overcome the opposing environments and break the arrows of the enemy.  
Today is the first Sunday of this month, and it is the first Sabbath as we enter the second half of the year after spending half a year, so please bless us on this holy day, Father. Please completely capture our bodies and minds within Your will, and hold us with the touch of Your power. Remove all elements of evil, awaken the essence of good, and let us experience a new history of resurrection where we can be embraced in Your bosom.  
I believe that Your lonely children scattered across South Korea are gathering here to worship You, so please be with them as well. Please clearly show that You are alive and that only those who are faithful to You will be victorious and stand in a place of glory on this earth.  
At this time, we gather all our sincerity to offer worship to You, Father, so may it be pleasing to You, and may countless spirits in the heavenly world respond and praise the day of liberation before You. Thus, please allow this altar to become a victorious altar where many spirits can ask to resolve their grievances on earth.  
On this day, please remember all Your children scattered across the world, for they are praying toward Korea even now. Father, all their sincere prayers and tears are for one purpose, to fulfill Your will, so please look upon all their desires and fulfill what they seek. We earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Father! The beloved young people who came from Japan are returning today, so please be with them and let all their coming and going be for the purpose of revealing Your will. Whether they stay or act, may it not happen unless it brings You glory, we earnestly hope for this.  
Please receive those who are working to bring all the people of Japan back to You as Your heavenly messengers, and raise them up to bring about a new history of resurrection on that land, Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Father, please newly command and encourage the lacking children gathered here so that this time may be a time to prepare for going toward the new world of promise without any lack. Please make us Your sons and daughters, armed with heavenly soldiers, who can run toward the enemy camp, we earnestly hope and wish for this.  
As we, the lacking ones, gather to worship, please embrace this one hour with Your grace, and start with holy grace and reap results with holy grace, we earnestly ask, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Prayer (II)> Father, we wish that all things in heaven and earth would eternally praise You, the Lord of all.  
There is not a single being that exists outside of Your connection, so all things created through You, through Your heart, raise Your glory and reveal Your holiness and profundity, showing Your infinite value, we know this. Among them, when You created humanity as the center of all things, You made us in the image of sons and daughters who can represent all things, combining both the internal and external aspects of Your whole.  
Human beings were originally meant to exist forever in Your heart and could not escape from the bond with You.  
All things also have a relative relationship with humanity within that bond, and they were meant to exist in a heavenly kingdom where freedom, peace, and happiness dwell forever, serving You and rejoicing in the eternal victory. However, we know that the origin of this miserable history arose because the ancestors of humanity fell. As a result, not only humanity became miserable, but all things became miserable, and not only all things became miserable, but even You, the Creator God, had to be placed in a position of misery.  
Father! We understand that it is our responsibility to completely remove all the conditions that led to the history of sorrow.  
To go through this responsibility, countless good spirits in the heavenly world are fighting on behalf of this earth with a hopeful heart, just as the good angels cooperated during the creation of Adam and Eve, looking toward the second foundation.  
You, Father, have been carrying the mission to restore the poor lives that move in the opposite direction from the direction centered on the angelic world, and You have been working against the sorrowful history until now, and the reason for Your hard work is due to the mistakes of our ancestors. However, it does not end with the mistakes; You are working hard to restore and see liberation, and we know that this is the history of Your effort.  
We must realize that if we do not establish a foundation of victory by carrying out the resolution of our individual grievances in any environment of the history we live in, we will become unworthy beings who cannot stand before Your hard work.  
We, who have inherited the traces of sorrow from our ancestors who left behind a history of sorrow, have gathered before You again today. However, we are lacking beings who cannot call You Father. We are well aware that we are the descendants of such unworthy sinners.  
We are those who cannot establish a bond of heavenly life and cannot receive the grace of resurrection, who are so unworthy and ignorant that we cannot stand before Your will. However, we know that You are compassionate, merciful, and the embodiment of love, and that You are in a position where You must call us even now.  
Knowing this, we have come before You with a shameful posture, unable to control our lacking bodies and minds. Before You, Father, we have come out with a heart that wishes to call You Father through Your heart, filled with tears of repentance. Therefore, Father, please come and raise us up with a heart of compassion, and grant us the special grace to call You Father through the bond of Your life.  
We wish to be able to call You Father, the Lord of all things who created heaven and earth, and to have ideals that align with You, and realizing this tremendous fact, we should return gratitude and glory before You, recognizing that we have no way to repay Your grace, we earnestly hope for this.  
Father, we have nothing. We do not wish to possess anything. We only have the dirty flesh and blood that have been stained by the traces of having received Satan's lineage, and all that belongs to us is under the domain of the enemy, so it cannot be offered as a sacrifice before You.  
Therefore, please allow us to become Your sons and daughters who can come to You with nothing but a naked body and a heart like that of a child.  
Please remove all the concepts we have held until now and everything we know. Let our knowledge, purpose, and life become entirely for You. Thus, in this time, please allow us to be in a position where we can serve and worship You. When You personally command, please allow us to have hearts that can willingly burn all of ourselves. We earnestly hope for this, Father.  
Father, we earnestly wish for You to personally preside over this time, and may You be with Your lonely children scattered across South Korea, worshiping before You. Please remember and protect Your sons and daughters who are fighting for each nation, raising the banner of unification across the world.  
Let everyone who does not know Your story feel sorrow and establish a heart of loyalty for You. Therefore, as they follow the great will, let them be prepared to face death, praising the bond of life, and let their footsteps, which strive to love beyond nations and the world, be protected, we earnestly hope for this, Father.  
May You testify that they are Your sons and daughters who are working with You and may You extend Your powerful hand to them so that they can be a light in this dark world. Also, may You extend the authority of resurrection before the nations. Thus, please ensure that they can fulfill Your desire to establish one world, and may they be equipped with the inner transformation of soldiers fighting for You and the external conditions necessary for this.  
Please look upon all the stories of their prayers and tears for the land of Korea with compassion. Please do not let their tears be in vain, and may their sorrowful tears not disappear from that land, we earnestly hope for this, Father.  
We earnestly wish that You would manifest at this time and speak to us.
I earnestly wish for this. I know that there is Your hand that must liberate all things bound by the chains of Satan in the world of death, and I know that the connection and protection of Your heart must be here, so please awaken us with Your loving touch. I sincerely hope and desire that You establish a connection that allows us to embrace the new flame of life in Your bosom.

At this time, I earnestly hope that You will receive everything within the purpose that You are orchestrating, and I ask that You allow us to become direct descendants who can remove the conditions of sorrow bound in history and resolve the grievances of the times, so that we can meet directly with You and receive Your commands for Your wishes.

Now, I dedicate this permitted time before You, and I earnestly hope that You will personally accept it, and I ask that through the words delivered from this altar, we may be allowed to connect with You. 

Father, please make the hearts of the messenger and the receiver one, and bind us together through the emotional connection that You desire. Thus, please allow us to become beloved family members who can be realized in our original form, and I earnestly ask that You permit us to become one family.

I earnestly request that this time be a promise to fulfill our loyalty for the glorious day when we can appear before You, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> At this time, I will speak on the topic of "Our Pride." We know that there are countless nations and ethnic groups on this earth today. 

Even when looking at a single nation, the desire to take pride in one's ethnicity is a requirement of that nation. Likewise, if there is a sovereign ruling a country, it is the wish of that sovereign to be a proud ruler who can boast of the nation's power to the world. This applies not only to a nation but also broadly to the world and individually to each of you. The desire to take pride in oneself motivates individuals to connect with their environment, their nation, and the world. This is human nature.
