Considering this, we cannot deny that the original intention of humanity, the living environment of humans, and the flow of human history all move in this direction. So, where did this connection and motivation originate?

If God exists and created heaven and earth, then God Himself must be in such a position, and all beings connected through God possess the desire to elevate themselves and reveal themselves. Therefore, we cannot conclude otherwise than that this is because of the Creator.

God also wishes to take pride in Himself. If we look back to the time before history, when the Creator admired the world of creation and rejoiced at the creations He made over six days, it is certain that God created all things because He had the desire to take pride in Himself through all created beings. No matter what created being we consider, such a story is intertwined.

In the created world you observe, or in nature, there exist various creatures. What process did all existing phenomena go through to be created? They were created through the heartfelt process of the Creator's sincere heart. No matter how insignificant a being may be, it was undoubtedly created through God's love and possesses the heart of pride that God desires.

From this perspective, you must understand that from the smallest insignificant being to the vast universe that we cannot fathom, all existing things were created as objects of pride that God wished to boast about.

You have lived centered around the created beings that remain on this earth. In other words, it is a fact that you have used and utilized all things, whether you like it or not. If all the things you use in your daily life were created for the purpose of God wanting to love and take pride in them, have you truly treated them according to their value? Ask your true heart. Indeed, how many people can truly do so? That is the issue.

When you wake up in the morning and look outside, the bright morning sunlight greets you. What does that sunlight signify? What is nature demanding of you? Have you welcomed that light with a heart that praises it as the glory of God and the marvelous gift of God's creation? If you have not lived in such a way, you must recognize that you become a shameful figure before the created beings that were made with such content.

Human beings, who should be the pride of God, were created to reveal God's pride in all things. Because God created all things with this heart, there must be a relative existence that can recognize and take pride in the created beings.

The reason for the creation of the angelic world is also here, and the reason for creating Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, or in other words, the protagonists of all creation, is also here.

When God created Adam and Eve, He thought of them as beings who could rejoice and take pride in the created beings that He wished to boast about. We must recognize this fact. Moreover, on the day when Adam and Eve, whom God intended to establish as central beings, stand as central beings before the universe, how much would God wish to take pride in them? To what extent would the limits of that pride reach? Would it be through only certain parts of the created beings? No. God wished for a day when He could mobilize all of creation to take pride.

Thus, humans were created as precious and valuable beings. God wished for humans to stand in a position where they can praise God's glory and to have a day when they can proclaim the achievements of creation before all creation. However, humans have not been able to stand in such a position. This is the grievance. If humans, who are in a position that has no relation to the content that God wishes to take pride in, are standing in a position that causes God to grieve, then we cannot deny that they are in a position that contradicts and opposes the original standard of God's creation.

Humans must first be beings who can take pride in God. They should take a position where they can say, "I have qualified as the owner of the universe on behalf of God." At this time, you have the responsibility to internally prepare and receive everything with a leap, yet if you find yourself in a position where you are all being swept away and falling before the incoming tide, can that person be a child of God?

Even while you are sleeping or eating, you must save time to deal with and overcome this miserable situation. Now is the time to establish the position of a child who has the authority to do so, yet if you forget this and become a group that cannot manage your fallen selves and fulfill your responsibilities, you will face destruction. However, because this is the multitude that God has sought through 6,000 years of toil, it cannot be so.

If you cannot achieve victory with this content and cannot boast about it, then your descendants will have to fight against Satan. Teacher like Joseph
The founder of the Unification Church, Reverend Moon, has been pushed to the forefront of the nation and the state while pioneering this path for 50 years. During the Japanese occupation, he faced the guns of the Japanese, and under the Communist regime, he faced the guns of the Communists. In the democratic world, he faced the dictatorship. He has emerged from the persecution of these three eras, risking his life.

Not only that, but the three governments of the Republic of Korea (the Liberal Party, the Democratic Party, and the Republican Party) have all tried to drive the Unification Church away with various persecutions, and even Christianity, which should have been our comrades and brothers in heaven, opposed us. Those who should have become our brothers and family, who came out first, have opposed and persecuted us to this day.

When I think that the voices opposing the Unification Church from established denominations have not ceased even now, I feel indignant and resentful.

The teacher thinks of Joseph at such times. Joseph fell into a pit from which he could only die due to his brothers, and was sold to foreigners and taken to Egypt. While working in the house of Potiphar, the captain of the guard, he was falsely accused and imprisoned, but under God's protection, he received grace and became the prime minister of Egypt.

At that time, there was a famine in all the land, so Joseph's brothers came to Egypt to seek food. Joseph, with his unjust and resentful heart, could have sent them away in anger, but he bit his tongue and endured, thinking of them as his father's blood and his own brothers. (Refer to Genesis chapters 39-42)

Knowing Joseph's heart, the teacher prays with that feeling. The Unification Church will not perish. Even if all kinds of accusations and arrows of slander fly, those arrows may be broken, but the teacher will not fall. Therefore, the Unification Church will not perish.

Until now, there has been no one on this earth who can stand centered on God's heart. There has been authority centered on the fallen nature, but there has been no authority that can stand centered on God's heart. The teacher knows this, so he has not despaired even in the valley of death, lying like a corpse. Even at the crossroads of life and death, where life and death are at stake, the teacher did not act like a coward. He has lived a life worthy of a man.

But where have all the sheep that have been prepared and equipped until now gone, and where are the goats? This is due to the nation’s failure to fulfill its responsibility. The established church should have repented of the sins of the nation and built an altar for God. However, because the established church could not fulfill its responsibility, the nation has become a people that is driven and chased away. Therefore, one must have a heart that loves the lost sheep more than the sheep themselves to save all the sheep. You must know that the teacher has endured until today with such a heart.

<Words> The ancestors of humanity were in an important position where they had to keep the command of God along with life in the Garden of Eden. That position was indeed more important than anything else. However, because the ancestors of humanity could not maintain that position, we know well that the history of humanity began tragically, bringing about a world of results that God did not desire due to the fall.
So what was more important for Adam? It was God's word and God Himself. Then what was the next important thing? It was the oneness of himself with God's word and God. If humanity's ancestors had started from such a standard, there would have been nothing better for us. If that standard had been established, God's word would be within us, and God Himself would also be within us. In other words, while God Himself is with us, we can also become one with God.

Despite such an important standard being given to humanity, the ancestors of humanity forgot that more important standard and brought about the less important result of the fall. Therefore, humanity, living in the consequences of that result today, is not standing in a more important position but rather in a less important one. In other words, we are not standing in a place where our hearts can rejoice and hope, but rather living in despair where our hearts are sad and devoid of hope. You are well aware that this is the world of such consequences.

God must save humanity, which has fallen into such a position, and humanity must seek to escape from that position and find the standard that was needed in the original world. Thus, the historical process of humanity has been a search for that path. According to God's providence, religions have been established on this earth, and humanity has sought God through religion. Thus, this world has now become the final world.

What humanity around the world must seek today is something more important than what was lost by the ancestors of humanity in the Garden of Eden. In other words, it is time to seek God's word and God Himself. You must understand that as we move toward the ultimate world, this becomes an urgent requirement.

So what is it that all of humanity is seeking in this world? What humanity has been seeking, even vaguely, until now is the inner, spiritual, and furthermore, the ideological and idealistic. In other words, it is not the external but the internal; it is not material but idealistic. Humanity is seeking these things.

What is the center of that idealistic, non-material thing? It is truth. Therefore, what has the history of humanity sought until now? It has sought truth. That is, it has sought an individual that truth aims for, a family that truth aims for, a race, a nation, and a state that truth aims for. This has manifested as a single ideology and thought globally. In other words, humanity has sought a new ideology that can connect to truth and a new world of thought centered around that ideology.

Therefore, you must not be detached from that thought and ideology, that truth. Your body must become one with that ideology and truth. However, it is not enough for the body to be one alone. We must establish the standard that was more important to us, which is to become one with God through God's word in the Garden of Eden. Without completely restoring that standard, humanity cannot resolve the more important issues.

So what is the ultimate point that can be resolved by pursuing ideology? It is God's word. In other words, we must understand that history has developed until now to align the truth that humanity seeks with the truth that God intended to establish, and that the aligned truth determines the standard for becoming one with God. The external world has also developed in relation to this standard of truth. In other words, the material world has developed as well. This is being contributed by science.

Then what is the ultimate standard we must occupy? It is the truth that God intends to establish. Centered on that truth, God and humanity must become one. In other words, unless the standard that Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, were to achieve in the Garden of Eden is fulfilled, no matter how much humanity wishes for it, they cannot achieve the purpose of that hope.

The history until now has developed toward this purpose. Thus, the ideologies and thoughts presented as means and methods to achieve the desired world are materialism centered on the material aspect and idealism centered on the spiritual aspect. Democracy has developed centered on the ideology of religion and culture, which is idealism. Humanity remains in a state where these two ideologies oppose each other. This is similar to the state of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, who were in the middle ground between God and Satan. In other words, you must understand that the boundary between parents born with the connection of nature and fallen parents, between people of nature and evil people, has emerged in the process of re-entering the original standards of Eden on a global scale.

How should humanity, which must become one with God, act today? Humanity must become those who seek the truth that aligns with God's command, "Do not eat," which is the word of God's truth. Furthermore, they must become those who can become one with that truth. Only when there are people who are one with the truth can humanity become one with God centered around that person.

The command that God gave to humanity, "Do not eat," means that while there is internal oneness centered on God, there was no external oneness. Through whom will that external oneness be achieved? It will be achieved through people. Originally, if humanity had not fallen, they would have become God, who embodies the external reality. By the emergence of a person who can align with God's internal truth, the standard that was internally unified becomes externally unified centered around that human. Only then can God Himself become the embodiment of truth, and at the same time, humanity can become one with God, equipped with the embodiment of truth.

However, due to the fall, this was shattered. The word that God established fell away, and Adam and Eve, who were to become one with God through the word, also shattered. As a result, the ancestors of humanity could not become the ancestors of goodness, and humanity became fallen descendants, thus lacking that standard. Therefore, according to God's providential will, He is seeking to find a single ancestor of humanity who can connect with that standard of truth through the providence of restoration or salvation.

Originally, if the ancestors of humanity had completely aligned with the truth established by God and achieved oneness with God, the first standard that God valued above all else and that humanity could value in the Garden of Eden would have been determined. However, the ancestors of humanity lost this. By losing this, they became divided into internal and external aspects. Humanity was to bear the external aspect, but because humanity fell, the external and internal standards became completely separated.

In other words, by losing the standard that could be unified internally and externally, the internal and external standards became divided from each other. As a result, heaven and earth were separated, and humanity and God were also separated. The earth and humanity, which were to be the original humanity and original earth, became results that were neither original humanity nor original earth. Therefore, when God looks, humanity is divided as humanity, and the earth is divided as the earth. Everything has been shattered.

The history of restoration to establish the standard of oneness between God, humanity, and the earth has been the restoration history that has unfolded to organize this world in such a position. However, because Jesus could not fulfill this and was opposed and driven away, there remains a resentment.  
To resolve this in reality, the founder of the Unification Church has been carrying out this work until now. Since 1960, how much turmoil has there been? The entire church and 30 million opposed it. Yet, he has loved them instead. Humans were born as children of Satan. They are humans in the world of Satan, but they must be loved.  
Because the archangel fell due to feeling a lack of love, we must not only love the sons and daughters of God.  

**Let Us Organize Our Families**  
**Summary of the Message**: With the determination of God's day, the center of the universe is determined, and everything returns to one.  
Those who do not know God and think of themselves as the highest will inevitably be broken. This is also the reason for the comprehensive movement of regional leaders.  
The spirit world corresponds to the angelic world, and blessed families correspond to the family of Adam. Therefore, we must restore the spirit world, and for that, the spirits of the ancestors must return.  
Until now, all ceremonies were for indemnity, but from now on, they will be centered on the principle of parents.  
The first seven-year course is the course walked by the teacher. Three years of the second seven-year course is a period for each person to stand in the position of their ancestors.  
You must achieve what Jesus had to do centered on family by establishing the twelve disciples and restoring the nation of Israel.  
From January to July of this year corresponds to a period of 7,000 years. During this period, the faithful and filial piety will be separated.  
Now is the time to organize our families.  

**Let Us Know the Time**  
**Summary of the Message**: A wise person discerns the time of providence and acts accordingly. Such people do not live centered on their environment but live centered on the time. God does not deliver prophecies based on the environment but based on time. Therefore, even if one does not receive revelation, a person who aligns with the time inherits the meaning of prophecy.  
Time and environment do not necessarily coincide. Therefore, one must overcome the environment and align with the time. A wise person is one who aligns their time with the time of prophecy, and such a person can become a global figure. In Abel's time, Abel had to subdue Cain, and Cain had to submit to Abel.  
A wise person lives in accordance with the time of providence.  
The nation of Israel could have become a global nation, but they could not accept the time that allowed for it. Until now, Christians have also looked forward to the time of the Second Coming.  
To be completely restored, we must go through the eight stages of individual, family, tribe, nation, world, cosmos, and God. God has laid the foundation for a global standard until now.  

The method for fallen humanity to approach God has varied throughout the ages. In the Old Testament era, it was through offerings; in the New Testament era, it was through believing in Jesus, the Son of God; and in the era of the Completed Testament, it is through serving the True Parents that one can approach God.  
To protect the physical body, one must center on the heart (space), and to protect the heart, one must center on God (spirit).  
The age of thought is the age of thinking.  
When looking at heaven, earth, and humanity, the center of the earth and the center of heaven is humanity. How can we achieve unification? We cannot achieve unification with materialistic communism centered on the body or idealistic democracy centered on the mind. The body, mind, and God must be in harmony for unification to be achieved.  
Those who believe in the Unification Church must rise above the previous standards of thought. There should be rumors that believing in the Unification Church drives one crazy. One should be happier to find that a father who had died has returned to life than anything else.  
My body and mind, my life, and the society, nation, and world I belong to must all be governed based on unification. What has been achieved in this way is the ideal heavenly kingdom that the Unification Church seeks to establish.  
There are good times for individuals. However, it cannot be just individuals; one must establish connections centered on the relative world. The satanic environment and the time of providence must inevitably align, so one must first align with the time and conquer the environment and the world.  
Therefore, a person who governs the environment based on time is a victorious person, while a person who is governed by the environment is a losing person. You must revolutionize the environment based on time. In other words, you must align the environment with the time.  
Our official course is the course of indemnity and restoration.  
By connecting three nations, one must be able to influence those three nations to receive a global blessing.  
For the members of the Unification Church, there is a responsibility to be saved from a Cain-like position and to save the Abel family (the Moon family remaining in the North).  
The temple is like the body of Adam before the fall, which is why Jesus came upon it. Jesus had to unite the families of Joseph and Zechariah to fulfill the will.  
The nation established based on worldly environments and the nation Jesus sought to establish are entirely different. Joseph is the resurrection of Jacob from 2,000 years ago. Therefore, the family of Joseph is the core of Judaism.  

**The Providential Significance of the Second Seven-Year Course**  
Only with the Messiah can families, tribes, nations, and the world be saved.  
The idea that Jesus must become a personal Messiah and a familial Messiah is the thought of the Second Coming.  
The second seven-year course is the period that replaces the tribal and national messianic missions that Jesus could not fulfill.  
John the Baptist was a cousin of Jesus. Therefore, he represents Cain before Jesus. Additionally, John the Baptist was a father figure of humanity who fell and was restored. For this reason, John the Baptist had to hand over everything to Jesus, who came as the True Father. The Cain-like family of John the Baptist and the Abel-like family of Jesus had to unite.  
Jesus had to marry and have a family. The fact that relatives married within the royal family at that time was also to align with such external times.  
Jesus represents the internal spirit world, while John the Baptist represents the external physical world. Therefore, the expectations of Jesus as a son-in-law and those of John the Baptist as a son-in-law had to unite for the spirit world and the physical world to become one.  
If Cain does not establish the standard of reality, he cannot restore his parents.  
In the past, Cain killed Abel with a stone, and again, John the Baptist, in the position of Cain, became the one who caused Jesus to die by not believing in him.  
The question is how to manage the providential course up to the national standard. The day this is managed will be the day heaven is completed.  
The 120 families are families established based on the standard representing all nations of the world.  
Jesus, who was opposed and driven away from the foundation prepared by God for 4,000 years, inevitably went to find the fishermen of the Cain-like Satanic realm. This was for the sake of providential love to leave behind those who could shed tears for Jesus even if he died. Thus, Jesus had no choice but to be led by Satan and face trials. However, because Jesus overcame that trial, he was able to start the second course.  
Jesus was externally driven away at the completion level of growth.  
Jesus came to save Israel but was driven away from both inside and outside by Israel. At that time, Jesus could have gone to the Gentiles, but if he did, the entire 4,000-year history of Israel would have been shattered, so he stayed and bore the cross. However, after resurrecting and achieving the hope of spiritual victory, he established the spiritual Israel by raising the Gentiles. The 2,000-year history of Christianity has continued because Jesus resurrected and established the spiritual second standard.  
Jesus failed at the level of rebirth, failed at the level of growth, and only succeeded spiritually at the level of completion.  
The fact that Israel became independent on May 15, 1948, signifies that a new era has arrived.  
The providence develops globally. Judaism and the Jewish nation, along with Rome, had to establish the expectation of a son-in-law centered on Jesus. Comparing the present with the time of Jesus 2,000 years ago, the Lord of the Second Coming is in the position of Jesus, Christianity is in the position of Judaism, Korea is in the position of the Jewish nation, and the democratic world is in the position of Rome. Therefore, centered on the Lord of the Second Coming, they must also establish the expectation of a son-in-law.  
While Jesus achieved only spiritual salvation, the Unification Church is a denomination that aims to achieve both spiritual and physical salvation.  
The current time is like when Jacob returned after completing his 21-year course and offered gifts to his elder brother Esau. Likewise, the Unification Church has begun an interdenominational movement for the elder brother denomination, the established church. And it is also conducting a victory movement to unite the democratic world.  
Before God, Judaism is the first son, Christianity is the second son, and the Unification Church is the third son. The third son, the Unification Church, aims to save the second son.  
Until now, we have been chased and driven away, but from now on, it is time to restore our dignity and authority and to be able to counterattack boldly.  
Members of the Unification Church must become patriots and loyalists and heirs of historical loyalty and filial piety. Furthermore, they must become people who can take responsibility for the world. Thus, the Unification Church must become the religion among religions, the living religion, and the religion that society needs.  
The course of the second seven-year course is the path taken to find those who were chased away before heaven and to save those who were not established by heaven. Also, the children of the Unification Church are mobilizing to walk the second seven-year course to establish the same standard that Jesus found without being chased away.  
**Now is the Time to Restore the Tribe**  
Now is the time to restore the tribe. Therefore, when other tribes are restored, the Moon tribe will automatically be restored.  
The reason the teacher has told you to make a full advance is that the time is now when Jesus had to find fishermen, make them disciples, establish a familial foundation, and make a full advance, and that everything is prepared on earth and coordinated in the spirit world to carry out a complete operation.  
The teacher established the standard for family restoration by giving blessings between 1960 and 1963. Therefore, the members must establish this standard from this year, when the second seven-year course begins, until 1970.  
With the standard established to achieve victory on earth, the ancestors who have endured for 6,000 years in the providential position can now carry out the history of the Second Coming on this earth.  
Blessed families must be fully mobilized. Once we walk the three-year course that Jesus walked, we will have fulfilled the mission of the tribal Messiah. If that happens, it will be as if we have walked the ten-year course combined with the first seven-year course.  
After three years, we will organize tribes.  
If you evangelize 12 people, you can establish a tribe. If you can only bring three, it will not be a tribe, so you must not complain if you fail to establish the conditional number of 12 and miss out on tribe organization.  
Blessed families should live centered on the expectation of the three positions. When a son is born in that family, the expectation of a son-in-law is fulfilled.  
If there are families among the three positions that do not have sons, they should be able to send their sons as adopted children to those families. However, if that family gives birth to a son, they can reclaim their own son.  
When Cain-like sons and daughters are established, they must be able to raise them and eventually send them off in marriage.  
From now on, there will be no persecution on your path of evangelism. Anyone who persecutes will perish. From now on, what you have sown will be harvested as your own.  
The teacher intends to bless as many people as possible who have been members for more than three years. Those who cannot receive blessings are beyond the teacher's control.  
To raise Cain-like sons and daughters, you must prepare meals even if you go hungry and preach the word even if you have to stay up all night. Just as the teacher has done for you until now, you must do the same for them.  

**The Second Seven-Year Course That Must Be Walked**  
If you can get through the end of the lunar August well, the communists will absolutely not be able to emerge.  
Those who have been members for more than three years and have not been mobilized absolutely cannot come to church.  
Now, those who cannot walk the second seven-year course cannot come to church. If they want to come, they must evangelize and bring the children of faith with them.  
To evangelize, one must understand the Principle teachings, must shed tears, and must put in sincere effort.  
Regarding the children of those who opposed us, it is acceptable to treat them more harshly than we were treated in the past, three times over.  
The three positions of blessed families should not exceed one month or three weeks without contact with each other. They must live centered on the three positions.  
For one season, one family among the three positions takes responsibility. In other words, each family should take turns being the leader and lead the lives of the three families, and even when building a house, it should be built so that the three families can live together. Therefore, the three positions are indispensable.  
Four groups of three positions combine to form one group, and among them, exemplary individuals become the leaders. Four groups combine to form one team.  
Jesus had to find three sons centered on the 40s. And he had to bless them over seven years.  
To establish a church, there must be at least 120 people.  
When a church reaches 360 members, it must be divided.  
Over seven years, we must evangelize 120 people to establish the church.
